Municipal Finance Bureau Clears Old Arrears of Land Tax

The land tax in various districts of this city used to adopt a "bundled guarantee" system. In the old Shanghai County area, after each collection deadline, the incomplete tax payment lists were given to the local guarantors (地保) to collect on behalf of the government. In the old Baoshan County area, the local guarantors received the lists a year after the deadline to collect on behalf of the government. The local guarantors were bundled on a yearly rotating basis and did not hand over the uncollected tax lists to each other. If a citizen had several years of land tax arrears, they had to pay to each of the local guarantors who had handled the matter, and only after the old arrears were cleared could they pay the new tax. However, the local guarantors were scattered in various rural areas and had no fixed office location or business hours, making tax payments very inconvenient. Therefore, many of the arrears over the years were indeed due to taxpayers being unwilling to pay, but many were also due to the inconvenience of the procedures. It is reported that from the Republic of China year 17 to year 22, the amount of land tax arrears collected on behalf of the government by the local guarantors amounted to more than 500,000 yuan. After the Finance Bureau took over land tax collection this year, it was deeply concerned that the arrears would increase, making future clearing even more difficult. Furthermore, according to the resolution of the previous National Finance Conference, it was stipulated that tax collection should not be carried out by roaming around with the payment lists. The Finance Bureau therefore submitted a request to the Municipal Government for approval to abolish the payment list method from this year onwards and instead have the various land tax offices directly collect the tax. It is also heard that the bureau has formulated a method for clearing old arrears of land tax in order to thoroughly clear the old arrears and facilitate tax payments for citizens, which has been approved by the Provincial Government for implementation. This method will be carried out in stages. The first step is to clearly check the payment lists held by the local guarantors and collect all uncollected payment lists. The second step is to set a deadline after the old arrears payment lists have been collected, and the various land tax collection offices will collect the tax, allowing citizens to directly pay into the treasury. By doing so, citizens will have a fixed place and time to pay their old arrears of land tax, which will be much more convenient. It is also stipulated that those who pay their old arrears within the deadline will be exempt from late payment penalties and will have one-tenth of the arrears reduced. Those who do not pay within the deadline will be detained for collection or have their property forcibly executed to collect the arrears and late payment penalties as a warning. The method for clearing old arrears of land tax is extracted as follows:

(1) The old arrears of land tax from the Republic of China year 17 to year 22 shall be cleared in accordance with this method. (2) Within 15 days after the approval of this method, each land tax collection office shall prepare a register for each district map, listing the following items year by year, and report it to the bureau for verification: A. For those whose payment lists have not been given to the local guarantors, the number of households and the amount of land tax owed shall be indicated; B. For those whose payment lists have been given to the local guarantors, the name and address of the local guarantor, the number of payment lists given, the total amount, the amount paid, and the amount owed shall be indicated. (3) Within 15 days after preparing the register and reporting to the bureau, each land tax collection office shall summon the local guarantors in each district to clear the accounts with the outstanding tax payment lists, etc., and the bureau shall send personnel to supervise. (4) The following items shall be verified during the clearing: A. The total amount of silver on the payment lists received by each local guarantor; B. Whether the total amount of silver on the existing outstanding tax payment lists is consistent with the amount owed to the land tax collection office. (5) All outstanding tax payment lists held by each local guarantor shall be collected immediately after the clearing. The local guarantor, the director of the land tax collection office, the tax collector, and the committee member of the bureau shall stamp each payment list on the spot, indicating the date of collection for identification, and the land tax collection office shall keep them in custody. (6) Each land tax collection office shall prepare a register for each district map, showing the clearing situation of each local guarantor and the total number and amount of outstanding tax payment lists collected, and report it to the bureau for verification. (7) After the clearing, the local guarantors shall still be responsible for urging collection. (8) The collection of old arrears of land tax shall be limited to three months, and each taxpayer shall pay into the treasury themselves. However, each land tax collection office shall still order the tax collection police to cooperate with the local guarantors in urging collection. (9) In order to facilitate tax payments for taxpayers, the bureau may, depending on the circumstances, temporarily set up land tax collection sub-offices in districts with a large amount of arrears. (10) Taxpayers who pay their old arrears of land tax on time shall be exempt from late payment fees and shall have one-tenth of the total amount of their arrears waived. (11) Those who still fail to clear their arrears after the deadline shall be summoned by the bureau in conjunction with the Public Security Bureau for collection, or shall be forcibly executed in accordance with the law. (12) If any local guarantor avoids appearing for clearing after being summoned, each land tax collection office may request the bureau to detain them in conjunction with the Public Security Bureau for clearing. (13) If any tax collector or local guarantor embezzles old arrears of land tax or engages in malpractice in tax collection matters, they shall be sent to the court for investigation in accordance with the law. (14) The embezzlement of old arrears of land tax by local guarantors shall be recovered from the local guarantor and the responsible personnel or guarantors specified in the bundled agreement, and shall be paid in full within a time limit, but the period shall not exceed three months at the latest. The recovery of embezzled old arrears of land tax shall be handled in accordance with Article 11. (15) Those who are responsible for urging the collection of old arrears of land tax and are negligent in their duties shall be punished. (16) Five percent of the total amount of old arrears of land tax collected shall be set aside as a bonus. (17) The bonus shall be calculated separately according to the old tax of each map and each year, and shall be distributed as follows: A. The local guarantor shall account for 40%, but only for the map and year of collection; B. The tax collection police and tax collectors shall account for 40%; C. The tax collection personnel of the land tax collection office shall account for 20%. (18) Those who are responsible for urging the collection of old arrears of land tax and are in one of the situations in Articles 12 and 13 of this method shall not participate in the distribution of bonuses. Those who are in the situation in Article 15 of this method shall be dealt with as appropriate. (19) The clearing of old arrears of land tax is a complicated matter, and additional personnel may be added to handle it. The expenses shall be submitted to the Municipal Government for approval separately. (20) This method may be revised by the bureau at any time for matters not covered, and shall be submitted to the Municipal Government for record. (21) This method shall be implemented upon approval by the Municipal Government.

China National Aviation Corporation Prepares to Open a Sichuan-Yunnan Air Route

Ordered Two Giant Aircraft from the United States

Expected to Open the Route in May or June of Next Year

In order to develop transportation in the Sichuan-Yunnan border area, the Ministry of Communications has decided to open a Sichuan-Yunnan air route, with the ministry allocating 250,000 yuan for operating expenses, and ordering China National Aviation Corporation to be responsible for the preparation. A reporter from the Xinxin News Agency inquired about the preparations from the company yesterday, and the details are as follows:

Test Flight Once The distance of the Sichuan-Yunnan air route is 216 miles from Chongqing, Sichuan to Guiyang, Guizhou, and 264 miles from Guiyang to Kunming, Yunnan, for a total length of 480 miles. However, there are many mountains and unpredictable weather along the way. Last year, the company sent Nie Kaiyi, Deputy Director of the Aviation Group, Huang Baoxian, Director of the Business Group, and others to fly a test flight, and the results were good.

Purchase New Aircraft After the last test flight, it was deeply felt that there were many mountains along the route and the weather was also constantly changing, so it was necessary to use a well-equipped and powerful land aircraft to be applicable. The company is currently planning to order two double-engine Parker aircraft or other more sturdy giant aircraft from the United States, but this matter is still under discussion and awaits final decision. It is rumored that the purchase of Sikorsky aircraft is inaccurate, as that type of aircraft is a seaplane and not suitable for land flight.

Open the Route Next Year After being ordered to open this air route, China National Aviation Corporation immediately began active preparations. The Ministry of Communications has decided to allocate 250,000 yuan for operating expenses. In addition to a small portion already received, the remainder can be drawn from the Ministry of Communications at any time as needed. The company is currently planning to purchase the new aircraft and transport them to China first, then conduct another test flight before officially opening the route on a fixed date. However, it will not be realized until May or June of next year at the earliest. At that time, after the opening of this route, it will conduct consultations with Southwest Aviation Corporation's Guangdong-Yunnan air route to handle joint transportation.

China National Aviation Corporation Stipulates Ticket Prices for the Shanghai-Guangdong Route

In addition to increasing the number of mail flights on the China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Guangdong route starting next month, with one southbound flight on Tuesdays and one northbound flight on Thursdays each week, passenger transport will also officially begin at the same time. A reporter from the Huadong News Agency has inquired about the one-way and round-trip ticket prices for this route, as follows:

One-Way Prices From Shanghai to Wenzhou, 70 yuan; to Fuzhou, 130 yuan; to Xiamen, 175 yuan; to Shantou, 200 yuan; to Guangzhou, 270 yuan.

Round-Trip Fares Passengers who purchase round-trip tickets will receive a slight discount compared to one-way tickets. From Shanghai to Wenzhou, 125 yuan; to Fuzhou, 230 yuan; to Xiamen, 305 yuan; to Shantou, 350 yuan; to Guangzhou, 470 yuan. The validity period of the above round-trip tickets is one month.

Baggage Fees In addition, passengers carrying baggage exceeding 33 pounds will be charged an excess baggage fee, calculated per pound based on the distance of the route. From Shanghai to Wenzhou, 35 cents; to Fuzhou, 65 cents; to Xiamen, 90 cents; to Shantou, 1 yuan; to Guangzhou, 1 yuan and 35 cents.

Shanghai Telegraph Office of the Ministry of Communications Receives and Sends Social Telegrams

Christmas and New Year Are Most Suitable for Social Interactions

All Telegraph and Postal Branches in the City Can Receive and Send Them

Since the Ministry of Communications promulgated domestic social telegrams, they have been well received by all sectors due to their low cost and rapid transmission. It is learned that the Shanghai Telegraph Office is actively promoting this method of sending and receiving social telegrams, and is providing senders with simple and convenient methods in various ways to provide preferential treatment to all sectors. The details are as follows:

Social Telegrams Are Particularly Inexpensive

Domestic social telegrams have now been adjusted by the Ministry of Communications. All telegrams exchanged between various places in the country that are of a social nature can be received and sent according to specific methods, but only in Chinese or English clear text. These telegrams are marked with "交際" (social) or the English letters SLT before the name and address of the recipient. The cost of these telegrams is extremely low. For Chinese, the minimum is 20 characters, and each character costs only 2 cents of a silver dollar. For English, the minimum is 10 characters, and each character costs 4 cents of a silver dollar. If the number of characters is insufficient, the cost will still be calculated based on these minimums. Beyond these minimums, the cost will only be calculated by the number of characters.

Most Suitable for New Year and Christmas Greetings

As the telegrams are named "social," they are limited to social matters. They can be roughly divided into three categories: (1) Congratulating the New Year, Christmas, marriage, birth of a child, birthdays, opening of a business, promotions, etc.; (2) Condolences for deaths, condolences for disasters and illnesses; and (3) Thank-you events regarding the above congratulations and condolences. Because the cost of these telegrams is particularly low, the text of the telegrams is limited to the above three types of matters and may not include other matters. For example, when sending a telegram to relatives and friends in a certain place to wish them a Merry Christmas and a Happy New Year, one can directly write "恭祝聖誕並賀新禧" (Wishing you a Merry Christmas and a Happy New Year) below the name and address of the recipient (for Chinese, the recipient's address and name are limited to 15 characters, and only 5 characters are charged), and include the sender's name. Such a telegram would only cost 4 dimes. The text is concise and clear at a glance. Furthermore, the Telegraph Office will uniformly translate all Chinese social telegrams into code for transmission. After the receiving telegraph office receives the telegram, it will still be translated into text and sent to the recipient. No translation fees are charged for this procedure.

Winter Solstice Social Paper Uses Color

The Shanghai Telegraph Office is making every effort to promote Winter Solstice social telegrams this time, and has prepared exquisite colored telegram paper specifically for celebrating Christmas and congratulating the New Year, in order to allow senders and receivers to increase friendship and especially love and cherish them.

Telegraph and Postal Offices Can Receive and Send Them

All sectors who need to send various telegrams or social telegrams can send them at the General Office at 200 Sichuan Road, 565 Minguo Road, Sassoon Building on Renji Road, 15 Avenue Edward VII branch offices, and more than 30 postal branches in the city, which is truly convenient.

Situation of the Creditors' Meeting of Jiande Bank

After Jiande Bank announced the suspension of business, it must be resolved by the shareholders' meeting whether to liquidate in accordance with the law. Therefore, it is only announcing the temporary suspension of business. The board of directors and manager entrusted accountant Pan Xulun of Lixin Accounting Firm and lawyers Cai Liu Cheng and Qu Yue to handle all legal matters. Accountant Pan and others believed that the bank had been suspended for almost ten days, and the creditors did not know the actual situation of the progress, which would easily lead to misunderstandings. Therefore, it was decided to hold a meeting with the creditors at 2:00 PM yesterday (the 17th) at the auditorium of the Shanghai YMCA on Sichuan Road. 226 creditors attended. Lawyer Qu and Accountant Pan will reduce losses as much as possible, so they will proceed with "fairness," "speed," and "economy." The funds received will be deposited in reliable banks. However, a detailed report can only be made after the accounts have been cleared. During the meeting, creditor representatives spoke to each other, and the main points were: some asked how to handle savings, some asked how to clear bills, and some asked about losses and directors, etc. Accountant Pan was allowed to report the bank's accounts and assets and liabilities one by one, and answered each question raised by the creditors openly. A detailed situation must be reported after a detailed review of the accounts. If the creditors formally convene a meeting and elect representatives, they can investigate at any time. The meeting adjourned at around 4:00 PM. However, since it was only a report nature on that day, the creditor certificates were not checked. Later, after the procedures are fully prepared, it can only be formally carried out after registering with the creditor certificate. As for the creditor side, they immediately discussed the method of proceeding in order to seek a quick resolution based on the facts. In addition, it was reported that after Jiande Bank announced the temporary suspension of business on the 8th, creditors such as Lu Zhaoji rushed to the law offices of Shen Zongyong and Yang Shaozhi and commissioned them to handle the matter, and requested to convene other creditors to jointly organize a creditor group. Yesterday, the bank convened a meeting of creditors to report on the bank's accounts, but the general creditors expressed disagreement and it is rumored that they will file a lawsuit.

Extorting Thugs Arrested by Police

French Flag Suddenly Hung on the Roof of the New World

Qiu Peilin Illegally Borrows the Power of Foreigners

The Court Has Already Issued an Arrest Warrant

Qiu Peilin, a wealthy merchant from Nanxun, previously leased land and buildings around the New World near Jing'an Temple Road from Cheng Linsheng, Cheng Zimao, and Cheng Ji. He opened an amusement park. However, because Qiu violated the terms of the lease, the owners Cheng Linsheng, etc., sued the First Special District Local Court to terminate the contract. After three trials, the court ruled in favor of Cheng, and the Civil Execution Office of the First Special Court ordered Qiu Peilin to vacate the premises by the 15th of last month. Unexpectedly, on the 14th of last month, a notice from the real estate department of the French-owned Baishanlong Foreign Company was suddenly hung on the iron railing at the entrance of the New World, claiming that Baishanlong had the right to occupy the leased land and buildings on Jing'an Temple Road, Xizang Road, and Baker Road, and a French flag was hung on the roof to resist the execution order of the First Special Court. This kind of situation of illegally borrowing the power of foreigners and resisting the orders of the national court not only damages China's legal rights but also insults the national dignity. If it is not severely punished, the credibility of national laws will be lost. Therefore, Cheng Linsheng and others hired lawyers Wu Zhiping and Li Zhaofu to file a complaint against Qiu with the Criminal Court of the First Special District Court in accordance with Article 384 of the Criminal Law regarding the crime of destruction, requesting strict investigation and punishment as a warning to others. Yesterday afternoon, judge Ye Shengchao opened the Fifth Criminal Court for questioning. The plaintiffs Wu and Li were present in court. After Wu explained the case, Ye declared that the case had already been publicly prosecuted by the police, and the court had issued an arrest warrant. Since the arrest was unsuccessful, an arrest warrant has now been issued for Qiu's arrest. Therefore, since the public prosecution came first, the private prosecution could not proceed. If the private prosecutor knew Qiu's whereabouts, they could hand him over to the police for court proceedings. Wu expressed acceptance, and Ye then announced that the private prosecution was rejected. The reporter then inquired with Ru Baoyi of the Legal Department of the Public Works Department. According to Ru, after receiving the report, the police department filed a public prosecution with the First Special Court in accordance with Article 384 of the Criminal Law. Because the arrest was unsuccessful, an arrest warrant has been issued.

Qu Guocheng Charged with Murder Case

Qu Has a Very Long Confession

Stating That He Absolutely Could Not Have Committed Murder

丨 Result: Released on Bail and Ordered to Surrender to the Local Court 丨

On January 2nd of this year, the body of a young man was found assassinated with a handgun in the Caijiazhai area of Longhua. After investigation, the deceased was identified as Xu Jinhui, a native of this county, 21 years old, residing at No. 72 Keming Road, North Sichuan Road, son of a woman named Xu Wan. After the local court's procuratorate examined the body, they ordered it to be claimed and coffined. However, in May of this year, Xu Wan suddenly accused Qu Guocheng, a Shanghai native and former clerk of the Navigation Administration Department of the Ministry of Transportation, of being the murderer of her son to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau. According to the accusation, the Public Security Bureau dispatched detective team leader Gao Wansheng, along with Chinese and Western detectives from the Jing'an Temple Police Station, to arrest Qu at his residence at No. 11 Yannanfang, 1603 Lane, Jing'an Temple Road, but they were unsuccessful. However, at 2:50 p.m. the day before yesterday, Xu Wan suddenly encountered Qu at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Laoyalu Road. She immediately called for Chinese detective Feng Xiushan and Chinese policeman No. 292 to arrest him and detain him at the Laozha Police Station. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the First Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Police lawyer Ru Baoyi explained the previous situation and said that the Public Security Bureau has now brought the case file. Regarding witnesses, in addition to Xu Wan, there is no other evidence. The defendant wrote a very long confession at the police station, explaining that for various reasons, he absolutely could not have killed Xu Jinhui. Therefore, the Public Security Bureau's request for extradition in this case should be handled by the court after investigating the evidence, and so on. Then Gao Wansheng arrived in court and requested extradition. The court then summoned Xu Wan to the case. She stated that she was 42 years old, from Pudong, and the deceased was her son. He and the defendant were friends. On the evening of January 1st of this year, the defendant Qu Guocheng and his cousin came and invited her son out to play. Because Qu often invited Jinhui out to play, spending extravagantly, she refused and did not allow Jinhui to go out. Qu then went back. Unexpectedly, at 8 a.m. on the 2nd, Qu came alone again, inviting Jinhui to go out. At that time, she was not yet awake, so she could not stop him. From then on, Jinhui never returned. When the local court notified her to go and identify the body, the murdered person was indeed her son. Because her son's departure was indeed invited by Qu, she filed a complaint with the Public Security Bureau, and so on. Qu Guocheng confessed that he and the deceased were classmates at the Nanyang Senior Commercial High School. He did not graduate and went to work in the political world. What the plaintiff said was all untrue. Because he had a foreign disease on his neck, he was admitted to Suzhou Guangci Hospital on December 24th of last year for treatment. He only left the hospital on January 6th of this year and came to Shanghai, staying in room 601 of the New New Hotel for about a week. During this period, Xu Wan came to the hotel and met with him, informing him that her son had been killed. She did not do anything to him. Later, he traveled between Guangdong, Shanghai, and Qingdao. When the police came to arrest him, he happened to be in Qingdao. Therefore, the plaintiff's accusation was completely false, and he hired lawyer Ye Fukang to defend him, investigating the plaintiff's previous accusation at the local court's procuratorate against Zhang Xiangguan for killing her son because the evidence was insufficient to prosecute. After the defendant went to the police station for arrest, he immediately surrendered to the local court. Because the investigation did not involve the defendant, he did not surrender. The reason for this accusation was because the loan was not successful, and so on. Qian Hongye, the head of the Criminal Court, reviewed the confession and ordered that the case should not be investigated further. Qu Guocheng was released on bail of 3,000 yuan and ordered to surrender himself to the local court's procuratorate.

Seized by River Patrol Police Chief

Strictly Arresting the Ship Owner and Others Who Fled

Around 5 p.m. yesterday, Zhang Kefeng, the chief of the Fourth Detachment of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's River Patrol Team, was patrolling the river with police officers Du Wentang, etc. When passing Pudong, they suddenly saw a Ningbo ship named "Jin Wanshun" sailing rapidly from south to north. Fire in Shenjing Lane, Ningbo Road

Five-Story Buildings Shared by 28 Families

Houses Completely Burned Down, More Than a Hundred People Escaped

No. 11 Shenjing Lane, 462 Ningbo Road, is a five-story Shikumen building, with the interior being shops, totaling 28, including Yuanyuhang, Xizuji, Zhenyihang, Xinfu Cotton Cloth Store, Xinfenghang, Wangchangji, Dajiqinghang, Jikang Ningzhuang, Hongxing Silk Store, Zhenhuan Silk Weaving Factory, Qianyuanhang, Yongchang Shenghang, Ruixinchanghang, Qiandahang, Wang Fuxinghang, Lao Jiuhehang, Wenfenghang, Qingfenghang, Lixinhang, Tianfenghang, Asia-America Tie Company, Dacheng Chemical Pharmaceutical Factory, Hengfenghang, Xinchang Taihang, Cheng Qingxianghang, Yuanji Silk Store, Rui Runyuanhang, etc. In addition to the shop employees, there were also those with family members, so the population was no less than a hundred. Yesterday morning at around 4:20, a fire suddenly broke out in the rear downstairs of the building. Because it was late at night, no one noticed. When they were awakened, the rear staircase had been burned. Therefore, men, women, old, and young all rushed forward to escape. At the same time, the residents in the front also woke up from their dreams and struggled to escape. Unfortunately, there were too many people and the exit was narrow. Therefore, a large number of strong employees jumped down from the upstairs, and the order was in chaos. The fire burned more and more fiercely. Because the building was old, it was easily destroyed, and in a short time, it spread to the entire building and became a fire pit. Fortunately, the Central Fire Brigade had received the alarm and quickly dispatched fire trucks to rescue. It was not completely extinguished until around 7 a.m. yesterday morning, but the building had been completely burned down. The loss was huge. The cause of the fire is unknown. Because the households in the building never cooked, all meals were contracted to nearby restaurants, and the fire started in the rear courtyard, which was empty on all sides, so it was very puzzling. Afterwards, the police sent detectives to investigate and summoned the second landlord of the building for questioning in order to investigate.

Nanny and Tenant Conspired to Abduct Girl

Girl Found in Changzhou

Zhang Wu's Testimony is Cunning

Li Shi, the 25-year-old wife of Liu Shaorong, a Macanese employee of the Dalai Bank, who was born in Portugal, lived with her husband at No. 17 Xianyi Lane, New Chongqing Road, Public Concession. Because she had no children, she adopted Zhao's daughter as an adopted daughter two years ago, naming her Aihua. The girl, now 17 years old, suddenly disappeared on August 24th of this year. Li Shi searched everywhere, but there was no news. She reported to the police and requested an investigation. It was not until the 14th of this month that Li Shi received a report from Xing Afu, a servant of her cohabiting woman Zhang Wu, that Aihua was now in Changzhou and that he had personally witnessed her. Li then took a car with Xing overnight to Changzhou and, together with the local Public Security Bureau detectives, arrested the suspects Wu Qiuting and the woman Mu Wanzhen, and seized the abducted girl Aihua, taking them to the Changzhou Public Security Bureau for temporary detention. She learned that the case was actually committed by Li Shi's cohabiting woman Zhang Wu. Li Shi then returned to Shanghai and reported to the Chengdu Road Police Station, which dispatched Chinese and Western detectives the day before yesterday to arrest Zhang Wu and her maid Zhang Wu, a native of Changzhou, and detain them at the police station. Yesterday morning, the police escorted the two women to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin prosecuted them according to Articles 257, Paragraphs 1 and 2 of the Criminal Law for the crime of enticement, and stated the case, saying that since the two defendants were arrested, Zhang Wu had denied everything at the police station, while Zhang Wu stated that at six or seven o'clock on a certain morning four months ago, Zhang Wu ordered her to send a girl to Changzhou with Wang Songnian. She saw Wang Songnian and a woman at the intersection of Mahe Road and Weihaiwei Road, and they took the train together to Wang Songnian's home in Changzhou, etc. Therefore, Zhang Wu was indeed an accomplice in the case. Now the girl Aihua and the other two criminals Mu Wanzhen and Wu Qiuting are all at the Changzhou Public Security Bureau, and they requested permission to prepare a document to transfer them, and so on. According to Li Shi, Aihua is my adopted daughter, and the defendant Zhang Wu is a tenant who moved in on August 1st of this year. The female criminal Mu Wanzhen arrested by the Changzhou Public Security Bureau is my nanny. The nanny and Zhang Wu are very close on weekdays and talk secretly in the room. Therefore, since Aihua disappeared, I suspected that this matter was related to them, but there was no evidence, so I did not dare to report it rashly. Moreover, the nanny wanted to resign and return to her hometown the day after Aihua disappeared. After I retained her, she returned on August 29th. Now I found Aihua in Changzhou after receiving Xing Afu's confession, and so on. When questioned, Zhang Wu denied the accusation, and her testimony was cunning. Zhang Wu also only claimed that she and Wang Songnian had sent the girl to Changzhou together, and her testimony was vague as to whether Zhang Wu knew about it. Judge Wu Tingqi reviewed the confessions and ordered the two defendants to be detained and re-examined in seven days.

Central Vegetable Market Draws Lots Today

Stalls to Open on New Year's Day

The Shanghai Industrial Trust Society previously ordered by the Municipal Government, in order to prosper the central area of the city, specially built a small vegetable market and more than ten shops at the corner of Minxian Road and Shiguang Road in the central area of the city. They have now been completely completed, and the shops have also been fully leased. The tenants, such as the Central Department Store, are urgently needed in the area. More than 70 stalls have been designated in the vegetable market, and merchants who have registered with the Society in advance have been extremely enthusiastic. Even for the merchants in the nearby townships and towns in the center of the city, they have exceeded the quota by more than double. The Society has politely refused requests from vegetable merchants in other concessions to set up stalls. Now, in order to be fair, the Society has decided to determine the order of the stalls by drawing lots, and it is scheduled to draw lots publicly in the vegetable market at 2 p.m. today. The market will officially open on New Year's Day of the 14th year of the Republic of China, and the Central Department Store will also open at the same time. After this, the residents of the area will find it more convenient for their daily needs of clothing, food, and daily use.

Municipal Children's Welfare Committee Merges with the China Child Welfare Association

To Become the Shanghai Local Branch of the China Child Welfare Association

On August 24th of this year, during the sixth semi-annual conference of the Japan-China Child Welfare Association, Pan Gongzhan, chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Children's Welfare Committee, in order to concentrate the strength of child welfare organizations, represented the committee and proposed to join the Child Welfare Association as the Shanghai Local Branch. On September 7th, Wu Tiecheng, chairman of the association, sent an official letter to the Child Welfare Association, stating that "According to the organizational charter of your association, there are regulations for organizing local branches in various places, and it has been reported that active planning is underway. This committee is the only organization in Shanghai that seeks the welfare of children, and its purpose is the same as that of your association's local branches. In order to concentrate strength, your association in Shanghai does not need to set up another branch. The city may use the municipal committee for the public association's local branch, avoiding one more organization with the same nature and cause, and the results of mutual cooperation can be more efficient. You should review the letter immediately and officially recognize the municipal committee as your association's Shanghai local branch. "Kong Xiangxi, chairman of the Child Welfare Association, after receiving the letter, considered the matter important and specially appointed a five-member committee to study and plan it. At the 69th Executive Committee meeting held a few days ago, they presented their opinions. The committee members present all believed that the Shanghai Municipal Children's Welfare Committee was well-organized and had outstanding achievements. They welcomed and were glad to hear that they expressed their willingness to join the association for cooperation, and unanimously approved the recognition and ordered the secretariat to reply to Wu, notifying him of the recognition and expressing warm welcome. From now on, the two major child welfare organizations in Shanghai have merged, and their future cooperation is very promising. It is reported that the Shanghai Municipal Children's Welfare Committee has officially joined the Child Welfare Association as the Shanghai Local Branch, but for the convenience of handling affairs, it will continue to use its original name.

Sixteen or Seventeen Year Old Boy Turns Out to Be an Extortionist

Mailing Letters No Less Than Four Times

Claiming to be Driven by Desperation

Chen Zhongxiao, 48 years old, from Shaoxing, owner of Chen Xinda Dyeing and Indigo Shop at No. 35, Xichang Lane, Daxing Street, outside Xiaoximen, Nanshi, has some savings and was targeted by bandits. Suddenly, on the 7th of this month, he received a threatening letter demanding 200 yuan, instructing him to send someone to the Xian Shi Company Cinema between 12:00 PM and 2:00 PM on the 10th of this month, with the person holding a newspaper in their hand. If the money was not sent, they would face danger on the street, and someone would be there to meet them at the cinema. As Chen Zhongxiao was not at home, having gone to Shaoxing for business, he received another letter a day later, stating to quickly send someone to the bottom of the middle chair in the ninth row outside the Daxingban Theater at Xian Shi Company, wrapping the money in straw paper with a torn Shen Bao newspaper as a marker on top. This money was to be sent by the 12th of this month, between 12:00 PM and 1:00 PM. Unexpectedly, the next day, he received a third threatening letter, stating that the previous two letters should have been received, but there was no news of the money. Therefore, they were again instructing him to pay attention to the bottom of the chair in the fifth seat of the 26th row on the right side of the Daxingban Theater at Xian Shi Company, following the same instructions as the second letter. If the money was not sent again, Mr. Chen was advised to be careful, signed by Wu Tianxiong. At this time, Chen Zhongxiao had returned home from Shaoxing and learned about the three threatening letters. Therefore, he immediately reported the above situation to the Ximen Branch Bureau, requesting an investigation. Director Li immediately dispatched the Detective Team leader Shen Wenda, Deputy Leader Fang Linggen, detectives Bian Wenguang, Jiao Baojun, and others to go in disguise, along with the relevant constables, Western Detective, and Chinese Detective Leader Li Shugui, to wait at the Daxingban Theater at Xian Shi Company. When the time came, no bandit appeared to make contact. Therefore, the detectives returned to the bureau to report. Unexpectedly, the bandit sent a fourth extortion letter the day before, stating, "Respected Boss Zhongxiao, the previous four letters should have been received, but there is no news of the 200 yuan. We are now instructing you to send the money to the Huangjin Cinema at the Eight Immortals Bridge in the French Concession, wrapping the money in straw paper with red paper as a marker on top. This money is to be sent by the 17th." At that time, Chen Zhongxiao presented the fourth extortion letter he received to the bureau for investigation. Therefore, Director Li again ordered Detective Team Leader Shen Wenda to lead Deputy Leader Fang Linggen, Bian Wenguang, and others to go with Chinese and Western detectives from the French Concession police to wait at the Huangjin Cinema at 11:00 AM yesterday. Detective Fang Linggen disguised himself as the contact person, using straw paper wrapped with red paper as a marker. Before long, a boy of about sixteen or seventeen years old came to make contact and was arrested and taken to the bureau. After questioning, he confessed to being Tang Liangmao, 16 years old, from Shaoxing, living in a small inn with no fixed address, previously an apprentice at the Xie Kang Paint Shop, but he stole 100 yuan and ran away, spending it all. Now, he is trapped in the inn with financial difficulties and was forced to write the threatening letters in the inn. After questioning by Director Li, he prepared a document to submit to the General Bureau for further investigation.

Major Fraud Case of Opening Gambling Dens in the French Concession Concluded

Each Defendant's Situation at the Time Was Questioned Separately Yesterday

Concluding Arguments Announced, Judgment to be Delivered on the 19th

Deputy Director of the French Police Department Raoboze (transliteration) received a confidential report in late November, stating that someone was spreading rumors that the current French Consul General Mei Liai was taking leave to return to his country, and the new Consul General would reinstate the Concession's market and allow the opening of five gambling dens within the Concession, soliciting "motion fees" under the pretense of applying for permits. The French Police Department immediately dispatched translators Jiang Futian and Li Xianyang from the Gambling Arrest Team, disguised as capitalists, to conduct negotiations with the fraudsters in Room 202 of the Dadongxin Hotel on Xixinqiao Street on November 30. On December 1st, they continued negotiations in Room 301 of the Dafang Hotel on Zhengjiamuqiao Street. After both parties signed a contract, the fraudsters Yang Yingchu, Wang Baiqing, Zhu Zhenhua, Cai Baoshan, Pan Shucan, Yang Dingguo, and suspects Fu Fengshan and Pi Xichun, a total of eight people, were arrested on the spot. Documents and contracts related to the organization of illegal societies were seized from Yang Yingchu and Cai Baoshan's homes, and they were transferred to the Second Special District Court for interrogation and investigation. On December 13th, Judge Sun Pengxian conducted a preliminary hearing. The police prosecuted Yang Yingchu and Cai Baoshan for fraud as a habitual offense under Article 368 of the Criminal Code, and the remaining defendants for fraud under Article 363 of the Criminal Code. After a brief interrogation by Judge Sun, he ruled that the two defendants, Yang Yingchu and Cai Baoshan, should be under the jurisdiction of the Local Court and adjourned the hearing.

Transferring the Case to the Local Court for Trial, the details of which have been reported previously. Yesterday morning at 11:00 AM, Judge Zhang Chaozuo, accompanied by Clerk Zheng Rong, specially opened the First Criminal Court for the hearing. They first asked each defendant for their name, age, place of origin, address, and occupation. Then, Police Attorney Yao stated the facts of the case (the wording of which was the same as recorded in previous reports). The judge then took the second to eighth defendants down for separate interrogation. Yang Yingchu testified that a month ago, a friend named Han told him that the French Consul was returning to his country and that the new Consul would reinstate gambling dens, and that he could find a way to do so. In mid-November, Wang Baiqing came to ask him and Yang Dingguo and Zhu Zhenhua to go to Cai Baoshan's house, saying that there were capitalists who asked him to find a way

to obtain permits. He told them that according to previous information, there were five permits, two of which had already been taken, and only three were available. On the 30th, Wang came to him again, saying that the capitalists wanted to meet him. He then went with them to a Cantonese restaurant across from Xian Shi on Damalu to discuss the matter. He heard that the capitalists could invest 500,000 to 600,000 yuan. On December 1st, at 5:00 PM, Wang Baiqing, Zhu Zhenhua, and Cai Baoshan came to call him again, saying that the capitalists wanted to meet him in person. They then went to Room 634 of the Wu Gong Hotel, where they saw Pan Shuxie, who said that Yin Dong had booked Room 301 of the Dafang Hotel and that they would go to negotiate first and then call him over. At around 6:00 PM, they called him to go to the Dafang Hotel, where he met Mr. Hong from Yin Dong (the disguised translator), who said that there was capital

of 500,000 yuan. He said that it could only be done if it was real. They said that preparations were complete and asked him to sign a contract, which Yang Dingguo drafted. After it was written, they were arrested. At the police station, they said he was a fraud, but he did not receive a single penny. He just wanted to find something to do after it was successful. Wang Baiqing testified that he met Yang Yingchu last year. This time, around the 20th of last month, Yang told him that gambling dens could be opened in the French Concession, and each permit would cost 45,000 yuan in official fees, asking him to find capitalists, saying that it was best to have 1 million yuan in capital, or at least 500,000 yuan, and that there were a total of five permits, two of which had already been taken, and there were still three left. On the 25th, he met Cai Baoshan and told him what Yang Yingchu had said, hoping to

work as a waiter after it was done. Zhu Zhenhua testified that he did not know Yang Yingchu or Wang Baiqing and only knew Cai Baoshan. On the afternoon of the 26th of last month, at 2:00 PM, he went to Cai's house to ask if there was any construction work. At that time, he heard that there were three club permits in the French Concession and asked him to introduce Yin Dong. The next day, he found Yang Guoding and went to Cai's house to ask. Cai said that the matter was real and that each permit would cost 45,000 yuan, half to be paid ten days after opening and the other half ten days later. On the 29th, he went to Cai's house again and saw Wang Baiqing. Wang said that they were waiting for Yang Dingguo and Yang Yingchu to arrive. Later, Yang and the others arrived, saying that they had to hurry up, or they would have to renegotiate after the 30th. Yang Yingchu also said that he wanted to copy the bank's deposit

account name and number and submit it to the authorities for approval, then find a place and issue a permit, and after it was done, assign him to take care of everything in the place. Yang Dingguo testified that Zhu Zhenhua was running a construction business at his place. On the night of the 26th of last month, Zhu came back and talked about the opening of the gambling den. He didn't want to miss the opportunity to find some construction work, so he found Pan Shucan to discuss the matter. On the 29th, he met Yang Yingchu, who was fully responsible. On the afternoon of the 30th, he received a phone call asking him to go to the Tiantian Restaurant on Sichuan Road to discuss the matter. Cai Baoshan testified that Wang Baiqing introduced him, saying that gambling dens could be opened in the French Concession and asking if he had Yin Dong. He replied that he would find one. The next day, Zhu Zhenhua came and said that there were three gambling tables, each costing 45,000 yuan, and

proceeded with the negotiations, hoping to be assigned some tasks after it was done. Pan Shucan testified that he only knew Yang Dingguo among the eight people and did not know anything about the police report of gambling den fraud. Yang Dingguo called him over and said that gambling tables could be opened in the French Concession, asking if he had any capitalists. He then introduced Pan Jihua, hoping to attract red-light business after it was successful. Fu Fengshan and Shen Xichun testified that they did not know the details of this case. They were called to the Dafang Hotel and were arrested. After hearing the testimony, the judge ordered translators Jiang and Li to report the process of disguised negotiation and then presented various pieces of evidence. After the court examined each one in detail, it ordered the commencement of arguments. Police Attorney Yao and the lawyers hired by the defendants argued with each other. The court then announced the conclusion of the arguments and scheduled the verdict to be announced on the 19th. Defendants Fu Fengshan and Shen Xichun were each released on 500 yuan bail pending further instructions, and the rest were returned to custody.

Spring and Autumn

Little Western Paradise

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Six: A Poor Girl Cannot Be Ashamed to Teach; Seeing Poverty in the West Is Not Enough to Induce Empty Humiliation

Auntie Hu said, "What kind of talk is this? Mr. Jia is asking you a question seriously, and you're answering him like that?" Jia Duocai waved his hand and laughed, "It's alright, it's alright, she's just shy, it's not that she's ignoring me. Coincidentally, I love it when girls are shy, you just be shy for a little while longer." Saying that, he laughed heartily. After laughing, he took out a flat cigarette case from his pocket. When Yueying stole a glance, she saw that the case was gleaming white, which was quite strange. Auntie Hu said, "Mr. Jia, is this case made of silver? How much does it weigh?" Jia Duocai said, "A little over one tael." Auntie Hu said, "Girl, listen to that, even his cigarette case is made of silver. One tael of silver is enough for me to eat for three months." Jia Duocai laughed, "If you compare it like that, what else can you say. Going east, it's very common to have a cigarette case made of gold." Although Yueying had heard her grandmother say how fortunate they were in their original hometown of Hunan, she had never heard of silver cigarette cases. She didn't expect to see one in person today. Because she was thinking this way, she couldn't help but raise her head slightly to look at Jia Duocai's hand. Jia Duocai was holding a cigarette in his hand, tapping it on the case, his eyes fixed on Yueying's face. When Yueying raised her head, their eyes met. Yueying immediately smiled and lowered her head. Jia Duocai then pinched the cigarette between his fingers and brought it to her, laughing, "Won't you have a cigarette?" Yueying raised her arm, blocking Jia Duocai's hand, and shook her head slightly. Auntie Hu said, "Silly child, silly child, even if you don't smoke, you should stand up and take it. Isn't this too impolite? Stand up, stand up." Yueying also felt that this gentleman was truly wealthy. If she sold herself to him, her whole family would survive. She should be more polite to this person and not offend him. (92)

A Sketch of the Reading Room

— Ji Jue

The university reading room is truly extraordinary. Whether observing it in terms of form or reality, it changes rapidly within the ten hours of the morning, noon, and evening, giving a sense of profound vicissitudes. As usual, the day's newspapers are delivered to the university, quickly distributed by the post office, and then distributed by the library for display in the reading room. After several turns, it is already past 9:00 AM. "Newspapers are the spiritual food of life." University students' love for this necessity is perhaps even more profound. Therefore, before the newspapers arrive, a group of people are already waiting in front of the reading room door, or even impatiently walking into the empty room, pacing back and forth. As soon as the library staff brings the newspapers and clips them in place, everyone rushes forward, each heading towards the newspapers they like, reading attentively, without any other movements. This can be considered a fleeting moment of the golden age of the university reading room!

A school community of over a thousand people is complex not only in form; each person's psychology, each person's preferences, and even each person's actions all exhibit great differences, creating countless variations. The changes in the reading room under these diverse conditions are only natural. Less than an hour after the newspapers are displayed, many gaps are found, and certain supplements have disappeared without a trace. That is the beginning of stealing newspapers. Friends who love literature target the supplements, those who pay attention to international issues and national affairs target the current affairs commentary and international news, and friends who love movies target the movie supplements... Each chooses what they like and takes it separately. Even "aspiring journalists" who study journalism clip out even the slightly more outstanding headlines.

Time passes, scene after scene, from morning to noon to evening. By 9:00 PM, the edible parts of the dozen or so newspapers in the reading room have all been taken, leaving only some unpalatable "chicken ribs," like incomplete corpses displayed on a battlefield, left for the library staff to do the "corpse collection" work.

Tidbits

— (Yao Kuangsheng)

On the road of life, the more twists and turns, the more flavorful it feels. If everything goes smoothly, it is not enough to display one's creative ability; the beauty of genius; a person who has not experienced hardship, how can they know the joy of joy? Living in a comfortable nest, one does not know one is blessed; it is like Pigsy eating ginseng fruit, eating without knowing the taste; it is like an ancient painting given to a farmer; a beauty given to a bandit; having a treasure, how can they appreciate and enjoy it; the life of such a person is missed, which is truly a pity.

Imperial Incense Drifting Record

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

After such a pilgrimage, not only was the Empress Dowager's heart extremely sorrowful, but even those of us with shallower relationships felt infinite sadness. Although people cannot escape death, their belongings often evoke endless sorrow in those who come after, which is truly an unpleasant thing!

After returning to her private hall, the Empress Dowager sat quietly to rest. The gloomy impression she had just felt was still lingering in her mind. We all withdrew, leaving only a female official on duty to attend to her.

I was also among those who withdrew to rest, but my body had not really been that active, so I did not feel tired at all. I only felt unusually bored in my chest and really wanted to relax for a while; unexpectedly, Guangxu added another layer of boredom to me. When he saw that no one nearby was paying attention, he suddenly whispered to me:

"I can guarantee you! In these old palaces, there will never be anything to commemorate me stored, no matter when!" As he spoke, he let out a bitter laugh that was even uglier than crying. "What do I have now? What thing can be said to belong to me? There will be even less in the future!"

After speaking, he covered his face and walked away softly.

Originally, the sky was still bright with sunshine, but now it was like being covered by a heavy cloud, and all that could be seen was darkness, sorrow, and gloom. (202)

Be Careful of Fire

Zhang Yuqing

The wheel of climate is constantly rotating, advancing into the winter season! The misty surroundings are only quiet and desolate. The mercury tube on the thermometer has shrunk to the lowest level, as if unable to breathe. The wind of December, the rain and snow at the end of the season, seem to be made specifically to invade the group of poor people.

Indeed, the weather is gradually getting colder, day by day, so cold that ordinary poor people are losing their lives, and even wearing tattered cotton clothes they are still shivering. However, noble people who do not come into contact with the air do not feel that the weather has turned cold. Perhaps because this year's hot summer was extraordinarily hot, exceeding the heat of the past sixty years, the beggars who borrowed the lower floors of the overhanging buildings as hotels were cursing God, why must there be winter on the wheel of the seasonal cycle!

"Cold winter months, be careful of fire," a few senior members of their group, thinking of this perennial business, returned to the sweet joy.

Indeed, this kind of business with no capital is truly worth doing. It does not cost money or effort, just circle around a few times at dusk when it is quiet, shouting "Cold winter months, be careful of fire." After a few days, they can go door-to-door to ask for money, and at that time, ordinary families who are unwilling to give alms will also break some money. Of course, having fulfilled the obligation, they should enjoy the rights.

From this, we must associate that if a person lives in society and wants to maintain their pitiful life, how difficult it is! Not only must they have a sharp mind and agile thoughts, but they must also have a considerable history and status! Furthermore, they must meet the needs of others.

Timely Gift

— Yue

The Story of the Little Coppersmith's Load

— Drunken Chi Sheng

The other day, Qing Quyu wrote in this publication about the gold wonton load, mentioning the Chen family of Sipailou in this city, who used to work as coppersmiths. Later, they became wealthy, and their descendants specially made a small coppersmith's load to be placed in the ancestral hall as a souvenir. As for the reason for their wealth, he omitted the details. I have a friendly relationship with the Cheng family, so I know it more clearly, so now I might as well talk about it.

The Cheng family's address is not Sipailou, but actually ××pailou. The house is large, with several rooms, all inhabited by the clan. Their ancestor, Cheng, was a coppersmith. He was diligent and thrifty. One day, carrying his coppersmith's load, he passed the door of a dilapidated household. That family had a few copper square bricks in the hall that they wanted to sell to him. He offered a very cheap price and exchanged them. When he returned home and looked carefully, they were actually all brilliant gold. He made this windfall, which was truly a joy from heaven. At this time, land was also cheap, so he acquired a lot of property. For a time, there was "Cheng half the city, Zhu a corner": this means that the Cheng family's property was more than the Zhu family's. However, by now, these two sentences are no longer relevant. Later, the descendants specially made a small coppersmith's load to commemorate their ancestors, which is still displayed on the gatehouse today.

World News

European and American Pawn Industry

— Fang Zhengping

European and American pawn industries can be broadly divided into three types: one adopts private ownership, such as England and the United States; the second adopts public ownership, such as France, Belgium, and Italy; and the third adopts a combination of public and private ownership, such as Germany, Austria, and Sweden. Here is a brief description of each:

(1) England

Private pawnshops in England are supervised by municipal and village self-governing bodies and must obtain a license from the Inland Revenue Office, paying an annual license fee of seven pounds and ten shillings. The interest rates charged range from 4% to 8% per annum, plus a handling fee of half a penny to one penny. The redemption period is one year plus seven days. After the expiration date, the pawnshop owns goods worth half a pound or less. Goods worth more than half a pound must be sold by auction. The borrower can still redeem the item during the period between the expiration date and the auction. If the auction price exceeds the principal and interest, the surplus should be returned to the borrower. However, within one year, if a borrower's pawned goods are sold at a loss, the loss can be compensated for from the surplus profit. The pawnshop is responsible for compensating for losses due to fire or negligence.

(2) United States

The pawn industry in the United States is supervised by the state governments, and the methods vary considerably. Generally, a fee must be paid and a license obtained before opening a pawnshop, and a guarantee must be provided. Interest rates are roughly divided into two types: one is based on the amount of the loan, and the other has a uniform standard regardless of the amount of the loan. For the uniform rate, the monthly interest rate ranges from 1% to 8%, with New Mexico being the lowest and Delaware being the highest. For the rate based on the loan amount, New York is the most well-known, divided into two categories: less than and more than US$100. For the former, the monthly interest rate is 3% for the first six months and 2% thereafter; for the latter, the monthly interest rate is 2% for the first six months and 1% thereafter. Other states, such as Maine and Virginia, also charge interest based on the loan amount. In addition to interest, handling fees are also charged for specific items. The redemption period also varies; some are explicitly stipulated, while others are agreed upon by both parties. The surplus from the sale of unredeemed goods must also be returned to the borrower. If the borrower does not request a refund, it is generally confiscated by the government. Pawnshops are responsible for compensating all or part of the loss due to fire damage, and some must take out insurance in advance to prevent unforeseen circumstances. In addition, charitable organizations establishing pawnshops are quite developed in the United States. They are specifically permitted by the state government to be exempt from business tax, which is also a form of encouragement.

(3) France

Public pawnshops in France originated in the early 19th century and were formally established by law in 1851. Private pawnshops were generally prohibited. The Law on Public Pawnshops in France was promulgated in that year and is still effective today. Public pawnshops have a board of directors, with the mayor of the town serving as the chairman. The directors are honorary positions appointed by the mayor of the city or county, and one-third are replaced each year. The interest rate on pawned goods is 3% to 7% per annum. The redemption period is generally one year. The surplus from unredeemed goods should be returned to the bearer. If the bearer does not request it, it must be retained for three years before it can be confiscated as part of the remaining property. In the event of a loss, the authorities are responsible for compensating one-third of the value of the pledged goods.

(4) Belgium

After 1848, all public pawnshops in Belgium were managed by the municipalities. The directors of the bureau are appointed by the mayor of the town or village. The operating capital is mostly contributed by the citizens. The interest rate on pawned goods is limited to 15% per annum, with a redemption period of one year. However, unredeemed goods must be sold thirteen months after the expiration date. The borrower can still redeem the item one day before the sale. For the sale of goods, 5% is charged to cover interest and handling fees. If there is a surplus, it must be returned to the borrower. Except for force majeure, losses of pledged goods are compensated by the authorities, plus half of the amount as compensation.

(5) Italy

Italy is the earliest country to have public pawnshops, and other countries have strived to emulate it. The capital of public pawnshops mostly comes from donations. The monthly interest rate is 5% to 7%; no interest is charged for goods worth less than five lire. The redemption period is six months, but the method can be changed to extend it to five years. Unredeemed goods can be sold two weeks after the expiration date. If there is a surplus, it must be returned to the borrower. (To be continued)

Education News

Chinese Social Education Society Agrees on Curriculum Standards for People's Schools

(Nanjing, December 17th) The Chinese Social Education Society believes that there are many people's schools throughout the country, and it is urgent to formulate curriculum standards for people's schools and publicize them throughout the country to meet the needs. They appointed Zhong Lingxiu, Gan Daobo, Yang Xiaochun, Feng Shaowu, Feng Guohua, Zhao Jiliang, Du Liangjie, and other seven people to draft them, and submitted them to the Board of Directors for referral to the General Assembly for resolution. They requested Zhong Lingxiu to convene the original drafters to a meeting. The original drafters decided to hold a meeting at the Ministry of Education on the 16th and 17th. Gan Daobo, Ma Shaowu, and Feng Guohua rushed from Wuxi. Chairman Zhong Lingxiu completely agreed on all the curriculum standards for people's schools, including Chinese, Arithmetic, Music, and Physical Education, and will submit them to the Chinese Social Education Society for submission to the Ministry of Education for approval and promulgation.

Simple Normal and Special Teacher Courses May Be Temporarily Exempt from the Joint Examination

After the Ministry of Education announced the regulations for the joint examination of normal schools, normal schools must participate in the joint examination this year. However, due to special difficulties and the simplicity of normal schools, they petitioned the Ministry of Education to review and approve the regulations. Those who followed the principles could make appropriate changes or postpone the joint examination. A few days ago, the Ministry of Education approved the postponement of the Shanghai Municipal Normal School Joint Examination. In the past two days, it also instructed the Hebei Education Department to handle the relief measures as proposed because the difficulties in the county normal school joint examinations stated in its report were indeed true. Yesterday, it telegraphed to the Jiangxi Provincial Government, stating that graduating students of the one-year simple normal course and the special normal course may be temporarily exempted from the joint examination.

Chinese Ethnological Society Established

Researching Chinese Ethnic Groups and Their Cultures

(Nanjing Communication) Academic circles Cai Yuanpei, Huang Wenshan, Ling Chunsheng, Sun Benwen, He Liankui, Xu Yitang, Yang Kun, Wu Dingliang, Chen Yinghuang, Shang Chengzu, Liu Xianou, Tang Zhu, Hu Huanyong, etc., in view of the fact that domestic academic movements in recent years, although booming, have not yet organized research on our country's ethnic groups and their cultures to meet the requirements of collective thinking and exploration, therefore, half a year ago, they organized the Chinese Ethnological Society. At that time, comrades from all over the country, upon hearing this news, were willing to participate. Now, the Society held its inaugural meeting at Central University in Nanjing at 8:00 AM on the 16th of this month. Members from all over the country who went to attend included Huang Wenshan, Hu Jianmin, Shang Chengzu, Qiu Changkang, Sun Benwen, Xu Yitang, He Liankui, Ouyang Zhu, Cheng Jing, Hu Huanyong, Wu Wenhui, Ma Songling, Rui Yifu, Luo Xianglin, and dozens of others. The Central Party Department sent Jin Maozu to attend the meeting for guidance. The meeting opened at eight o'clock, and the ceremony was performed as usual. Sun Benwen was publicly elected as chairman, and Ma Songling was elected as recorder. The purpose of organizing the Society was announced, followed by He Liankui reporting on the preparations. Then, the attendees gave speeches on their daily research experiences. Finally, various rules and regulations were passed, and supervisors and directors were elected. Those elected were Cai Yuanpei, Huang Wenshan, He Liankui, Ling Chunsheng, Xu Yitang, Shang Chengzu, Sun Benwen, Qiu Changkang, Hu Jianmin, Cheng Jing, and other nine people. The meeting adjourned at twelve o'clock.

Number of Students Studying in Japan Increases Sharply, Many Did Not Go Through the Procedures Set by the Ministry

Qualifications and Economy Are Currently Serious Problems

Zhou Xianwen Discussed Alternative Methods with the Ministry of Education

According to a survey by the Japan-China Academic Association, the total number of Chinese students studying in Japan this year is more than 2,300, which is double the number last year. A reporter from the Shanghai News Agency inquired about the reasons for the sharp increase from the Universal Student Association in this city yesterday, as well as the situation where the procedures for going abroad did not comply with the regulations set by the Ministry, as follows:

Reasons for the Sharp Increase in the Number of Students Studying in Japan The reason for the sharp increase in the number of students studying in Japan is the depreciation of the Japanese yen. Before 1922 and 1923, each Japanese yen was worth more than two yuan in national currency, but now each Japanese yen is only worth more than eighty cents in national currency, a big difference. Generally poorer students in our country believe that this is a great opportunity, so they go to Japan one after another to pursue further studies. Among the more than 2,000 students who went to Japan this year, most entered Waseda University and Meiji University. The subjects they study are mostly social sciences.

Departure Procedures Not in Accordance with Ministry Regulations The procedures originally set by the Ministry of Education for students studying in Japan required graduation from a school above the specialized level and a deposit of two years' worth of expenses in the Bank of Communications. A certificate must be issued by the bank before a study abroad certificate can be obtained. Among the students studying in Japan this year, many did not meet the Ministry of Education's regulations in terms of qualifications and economy. Therefore, most did not go through the procedures set by the Ministry for going abroad, and often went directly to Japan. This is currently a serious problem. Zhou Xianwen, the supervisor of students studying in Japan, previously returned to China to discuss alternative methods with the Ministry of Education, but it has not yet been resolved.
