Page 15

Free Talk

Newcomers to the Japanese Literary Scene in 1934

— Fan Hai

The newcomers who have emerged in the Japanese literary scene this year include Kenkichi Shimaki, Koroku Hirata, Kazuo Sasaki, Hiroshi Aso, Shoichi Hashimoto, Kazuo Shimada, Maki Fujishima, Rokuro Kusakari, Naoe Sugiyama, Yang Kui, Seiji Kimura, Shigeko Shoji, etc.

Among these newcomers, the most successful are Kenkichi Shimaki and Koroku Hirata. Kenkichi Shimaki's "Prison" can be said to be the most important work of the Japanese literary scene in 1934. As soon as he emerged, he immediately received great praise in the Japanese literary scene. The other five articles attached to "Prison," "Leprosy," "Blindness," "Depression," "Falling," and "Doctor," are all model descriptions of prison life. Therefore, Kenkichi Shimaki can be said to be the first famous newcomer in the Japanese literary scene this year.

Standing alongside Kenkichi Shimaki to become the two pillars of the Japanese literary scene this year is Koroku Hirata. He is the only representative of Japanese peasant literature in 1934. Originally, the bankruptcy of Japanese villages had fallen into an extremely tragic situation. Therefore, this year's Japanese literary scene was almost entirely filled with articles describing rural villages, and peasant literature was almost the main aspect of Japanese literature in 1934, and the most outstanding of peasant literature was Koroku Hirata.

Kazuo Sasaki is the farmer among the farmer writers. His "After the Fall" is undeniably the healthiest work. He himself is from a rural village. He breathes in the soil, fertilizer, and sweat, and writes heavy but simple and clear works by farmers themselves.

Hiroshi Aso co-authored "Boy" with Hayashi Fusao. The so-called co-authoring is rare in literary circles in various countries, and this is also worth commemorating in the Japanese literary scene this year.

Kazuo Shimada published a work entitled "Dung Street." The protagonist is the secretary of a free labor union, said to be the author himself. He wrote this work with considerable ambition.

Maki Fujishima, also translated as Maki Fujishima, is obviously a woman's name. She published "Life" and "Red Peeling." It is rare to see women who use such thick lines to describe their works.

There is another special phenomenon in the Japanese literary scene this year besides peasant literature, and that is literature describing colonies. In Japan, there has always been literature describing colonies, but the meaning of works written by the colonists themselves has only gained a deeper meaning this year. Here, Yang Kui and Rokuro Kusakari are representative writers. Yang Kui describes Taiwanese farmers, and Rokuro Kusakari describes Korean laborers. These two writers who describe the lower classes of Japanese colonies will give the Korean writer Jang Hyuk-ju, who is gradually moving towards describing the petit bourgeois life, a stronger intention, right?

Finally, Naoe Sugiyama is also a female writer. She is also a female worker in a cotton yarn factory. At a time when the Japanese literary scene this year is full of literature describing farmers, there is almost only one writer who describes factory laborers, Naoe Sugiyama. Therefore, Naoe Sugiyama is also a special force in the Japanese literary scene this year. Her description of the working conditions in the factory is so clear, varied, and non-repetitive that it is truly commendable. Up to now, there are not many writers who come from laborers who can describe the working conditions in the factory as accurately as she does, and report the ordinary and interesting one day in the factory without special accidents. Not only are there no traces of conceptual political doctrine in her works, but also no sentimentality and emotional excitement, which are unique to female writers. Among the newcomers, this writer is one of the most promising.

Tokyo Night Market

— Wei Zhongtian

Before I went to Tokyo, I had heard about how lively the Tokyo night market was. After arriving in Tokyo, I went to see it myself and felt that it was still "worthy of the name." However, I have not been to Tokyo for many days, so I have only visited the night market three times. The first two times, I just "looked at the flowers on horseback" with Lao Yu and came back after a while. The third time, I visited with Lanbao, Yaoman, etc. for a long time, and I also bought a little something. There are night markets in every lively place in Tokyo, such as Asakusa, Ginza, Shinjuku, etc. I am only talking about the night market in Shinjuku here.

I remember that on a Saturday evening the week before, after dinner, our group took the train from Higashi-Nakano Station with excited emotions and ran towards our destination. Probably because it was a Saturday night, the carriages were more crowded with people than usual. The train arrived at Shinjuku after two stops. People felt different when they walked out of the station. Everywhere there were red lights, green lights, purple lights, and incandescent lights, flashing, flying, and jumping. Cars were walking in formation on the road like black ants. The pedestrians on both sides of the sidewalk squeezed me and I squeezed you. It was really what they called "watertight."

The sides of the road are filled with many small stalls. Each small stall has a cloth awning, selling daily necessities and children's toys, etc. There are also cheap second-hand books, oil paintings, and picture cards, etc. We stopped in front of an oil painting stall.

"Buy a few oil paintings!" Lanbao said, and after saying that, she squatted down and flipped through them one by one.

I saw that the price was cheap and the oil paintings were good, so I bought four, and Lanbao bought two. One of the ones I bought was of three children. Lanbao said it was very good to wash their feet by the creek, so I gave it to her.

We walked slowly, looking at all kinds of things. It was really like the commander-in-chief reviewing the troops. Suddenly we saw a beggar sitting on the roadside. Yao said, "There is a beggar here!" She said with a bit of a rare tone. Really, we only saw this beggar after we arrived in Tokyo. Moreover, he was disabled. Although there are tens of thousands of poor people in Japan, there are very few beggars. Compared with Shanghai, Shanghai is too ashamed!

As we walked, we bought many fun things. Lanbao bought a little foreign doll. She said with a smile, "There is already a foreign doll in my house. I am afraid she is lonely, so I bought this one to accompany her!" This sentence made Fatty Sister laugh so hard that her eyes were like black lines.

Walking, walking, walking many roads, we also went to big companies, and we also went to the basement. We didn't return until around nine o'clock.

"The Tokyo night market is lively and charming!" I am thinking this now.

"Watching Cars"

— TK

Cowpox and Anesthesia

— Qiao Feng

Before mankind had writing or historical records, they had already discovered and invented many useful things and methods, such as the use of fire, the method of making fire, tools, and many things such as medicinal materials for treating diseases. If they were all written down one by one, the list would be very long. After there was written history, things that were beneficial to mankind were discovered one after another, and new tools were invented at any time. The method of vaccinating against cowpox and anesthesia are just two of the many in the middle, but their benefits are great. There is a reason to bring them up here to talk about them.

In recent days, I have seen papers posted on the road or in cars calling on people to get vaccinated against cowpox, which shows that smallpox is coming again. Smallpox is a contagious disease, and it is a life-threatening disease. It is widespread and the number of deaths is extremely high. It often becomes popular every spring; it is dangerous for children to be infected, and even if they are not infected, it is still a worrying thing; because people who have not had smallpox will still be infected in the future, and the danger cannot be avoided. Therefore, before the invention of cowpox, many places used smallpox scabs to plug their nostrils, so that children would be infected with smallpox once during the specified period. However, the method of vaccination cannot eliminate the dangers of smallpox, although it is slightly lighter. This danger was only removed after the method of cowpox vaccination was invented.

The discoverer of cowpox was Jenner, during the period of 1798. Jenner's name was Edward, born in 1749 (died in 1823), and was a doctor in Gloucestershire, England. Gloucestershire is a place where many cattle are raised, and cattle can also develop a disease similar to smallpox. When they get this disease, blisters appear on the breasts. People who milk cows sometimes get infected, but they only find mild symptoms, and then they do not get infected with smallpox. Therefore, there is a belief among milkers in Gloucestershire: that after being infected with cowpox, one can prevent smallpox. Jenner grew up there, so he naturally knew this situation in detail.

When Jenner was twenty-one years old, he ran to London to study medicine and studied anatomy under the guidance of Hunter. Hunter was a Scotsman and was an extremely famous star in anatomy and surgery. Jenner told Hunter that cowpox could prevent smallpox infection. But Hunter was too busy to study this issue. Therefore, the experimental research fell on Jenner's shoulders.

After he studied medicine, he came to study the beliefs of the milkers in his hometown. Through his experiments and research, he firmly believed that inoculating cowpox serum into the human body had very mild symptoms, but it could prevent smallpox. In 1796, he inoculated cowpox into the human body, and only mild symptoms developed, and then he recovered to health. He then took smallpox and inoculated it into the same person, but smallpox did not occur. This made him even more believe that cowpox could prevent smallpox. Two years later, in 1798, he published his great discovery and told the world.

In recent years, the method of introducing cowpox vaccination has become very popular, and smallpox is much rarer than before. Moreover, it is known that cowpox is not a mysterious thing, but a variant of smallpox. It is because the microorganisms of smallpox are reduced in their intensity after passing through the cow's body, and then inoculated into the human body, so that dangerous symptoms do not occur, but the body can also produce antitoxic effects to resist the growth of smallpox microorganisms. If human smallpox is inoculated into young female cows or rabbits, they can also develop cowpox, which can prove that what I said before is correct.

Camel Bells

— Zi Gang

A friend in the South Country wrote saying that, for some unknown reason, he often saw groups of camels walking in the endless desert in his dreams. When the wind came, the air was filled with dust and sand, and the heavy, turbid camel bells echoed in the air. These dreams, one after another, led him into a world of illusion, and the sound of camel bells seemed to be constantly ringing in his ears all day long.

Yes, in the early morning, before dawn, these yellow, massive friends followed their masters, setting off in the early chill, one after the other, silently taking heavy steps, carrying hundreds of pounds of burden on their backs: coal, lime, firewood… In addition to these, there were also bags of dry grass and small bags of steamed buns, which were the food the animals knew belonged to their masters. After walking a long distance, both the camels and the people were hungry, and they would stop silently. Their four furry legs lightly brushed away the dust, and their front knees knelt down. As soon as the masters put the food in front of them, their dull, thick lips began to move, and their eyes stared intently at the sky.

The bells under their necks rang. Besides the sound of the camels chewing and the masters coughing as they swallowed dry food, this was the only sound. This tone gently rippled and spread out like water patterns, entertaining the animals themselves and entertaining the masters, whose faces were full of wind and frost as they chewed and swallowed.

When they encountered another team, everyone waved their whips. The masters, like captains of a cavalry troop, exchanged smiles with their colleagues in a majestic manner.

“Setting off early, eh? Oh, these are really good animals!” The camel drivers always carefully examined other people's animals, just like knights admiring their horses.

"A hundred and ten or so yuan per head!" With the ear flaps on their leather hats flipped up, they walked past proudly, as if showing off their family wealth, just like calculating "how many heads of cattle and sheep," which was also a form of private property.

Some camel drivers were merely hired laborers, without any animals of their own, and worked for others. In this type of camel team, one would not hear many camel bells. They were almost omitted, or could only be found under the necks of the leading animals in the team. Thus, the entire team of people and animals slowly moved forward, listening to this single rhythm. On the raised humps,麻布 sacks or rope nets swayed.

"Hush!" The whip was waved in the air, and the feet that had gradually slowed down sped up again, as if they had put on full power.

If it were summer, the hardworking animals and hardworking people would be hesitant under the scorching sun. The animals each carried heavy burdens, while the people held heavy hearts and heads dripping with sweat. The sound of the camel bells seemed a bit agitated.

Only in winter, when the breath of people and animals floated in the air like white smoke, the swaying of the camel bells warmed their tired hearts.

This sound wave implied a firm and laborious journey.

Tomorrow (19)

— Written by (Joseph Conrad), Translated by Wu Xiangyu

"He leaned forward bravely. A little pale: this face suits some people. But you have the very beautiful figure of a girl, Miss Bessan."

She was completely panic-stricken again. Because no one had ever said so much to her before.

His tone changed again. "But I'm hungry enough, haven't had breakfast today. Can you find me some bread from where the tea is kept, or-"

She was already gone. He had almost asked her to come in. What did it matter? Anywhere would do. Damn it, now he was in a dilemma. What would his companions think he was doing?

"I'm not begging you like a beggar," he said humorously, taking a slice of buttered bread from the plate she held out to him. "I'm asking you like a friend. My father, you know, is rich."

"He is willing to starve for your sake."

"But I'm starving because of his strange ideas," he said, picking up another slice of bread.

"Everything he has in this world is for you," she retorted.

"Yes, if I came here to live like a punished toad sitting in a hole. Thank you; what would happen if a kick landed on my head? He always has his strange ways of showing love."

"I can wake him up in a week," she suggested timidly.

"He couldn't answer her because he was too hungry; she respectfully held the plate close to his hand, and began to whisper in a quick, anxious voice, just so he could hear. He listened, somewhat surprised, while his chewing gradually slowed down, until finally, his jaws stopped completely. That's his trick, is it?" he said in a very contemptuous, elevated tone. An uncontrollable wave of his arm sent the plate flying from her fingers. He cursed loudly.

She recoiled from him, leaning her hand against the wall.

"No," he said angrily. "He hopes! Hopes I-take his stinking money! ... Who wants his home? Crazy-isn't he! Don't you think so? He has his ideas. He used to want to make me a poor clerk, a lawyer, and now he wants to make me a cursed, caged, docile rabbit. Make me! Make me!" His forced, suppressed, angry laughter surprised her.

"I tell you, the whole world isn't too big for me to fit into-what are you calling? - Bessan-let a person stay coldly in that rabbit-hutch of a drawing-room. He wants me to marry and settle down! And seems to have found a woman for me-terrible to the extreme! Do you know 'Gide' (the woman of 'Punch' in the puppet show, a woman with a funny face), may I ask you?"

Her whole body trembled with silent, inner sobbing; but he did not notice her pain because of his excessive anger and agitation. He was extremely angry and contemptuous of such ideas. A window upstairs banged open again.

"A joke-seeking messenger," old Hagerbot announced decisively at the window in a firm voice. His voice, it seemed to Bessan, made the night itself turn mad - pouring madness and misfortune upon the earth. "Now I know what's wrong with the people here, my dear. Ah, of course. With this mad fellow running around. Don't pay attention to him, Bessan. Bessan, I say!"

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, the market conditions for each month generally showed a stable and revolving trend. The quotation for foreign wheat was slightly down by two jiao for Chicago near-term and about eight fen for far-term, while Canada was down by two to three jiao. When the opening price was quoted for foreign wheat, public sentiment was flat. Subsequently, due to the continued absorption by large bulls, the market held steady. However, as the settlement was near, the buying and selling by all parties was limited, so there was little excitement. By the time the market opened in the afternoon, the near and far terms were all firm. This month's term was due to the slight disposal of spot goods by the Tianjin customer group, who heard that the delivery in Tianjin was offered at 5.5 jiao, which was much cheaper than the standard. In the far term, the exchange rate was shrinking due to the continued entry of large traders, so public sentiment gradually rose. Observing the subsequent steps, it is feared that a fall will be difficult to achieve. As a result, this month's term recovered by 1.25 fen compared to the previous week, January was up by 2 fen, February was up by 2.25 fen, March was up by 1.5 fen, April was up by 2.25 fen, and May was up by 2 fen.

Forward Wheat Market Rises Slightly

Yesterday, after the opening of the forward wheat market in the morning and afternoon, the market conditions for each month showed a stable and firm trend. The quotation for foreign wheat was slightly down by eight fen to two jiao for Chicago and about two to three jiao for Canada. When the opening price was quoted, this month's term was flat in both the morning and afternoon transactions due to the approaching end, and there was little change in price. As for the far-term months, the morning was generally calm, but in the afternoon, as the market turned active, the buying interest was slightly stronger, and the opening prices for each month gradually became firm. As a result, this month's term remained unchanged, January rose by 2 fen, February rose by 3 fen, March rose by 2 fen. The current wheat market has once again become a bottleneck. Although dealers have opened prices, factories have no intention of allocating purchases, so there is no quotation.

Chicago wheat, Europe is unhealthy, and the Amal wheat harvest is approaching, and the supply will be inexhaustible. Buyers here are hesitant, and it is expected that the market will not undergo major changes in the coming days.

Three Ships of Foreign Rice Arrive

One Ship of Siamese Rice Sinks in the Port

Yesterday's foreign rice market situation was soft in the morning due to the arrival of large batches of fixed orders. Local customers were very sluggish, but after noon, inland areas competed for broken rice, while this street handled Saigon Siamese machine rice, and the market situation immediately turned around, and the market price gradually increased by five fen. A total of more than 1,000 bags of broken rice and machine rice were traded. New fixed orders arrived from Saigon in two ships, the company ships Pinawin and Aerete Mara, which were imported and are now docked at Yitaixingji, with a total of more than 50,000 bags. In addition, the Norwegian ship Harvard, loaded with 15,445 bags (1,500 tons) of Siamese rice, was sunk by the Tongde round in Lujiazi when it was imported yesterday morning. As a result, all Siamese machine-broken rice in the market became firm.

There is a slight stock of Ke Xian rice in the market, and arrivals continue to arrive at the end. The local customers are active in selling, and the market remains flat. Yesterday, Wuxi and Zhejiang inland areas handled 1,300 bags, and this street handled 1,700 bags. The market price is no different from the previous market.

He Xia is Mainly Strong but Prices Fall by a Jiao or So

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, sources from all groups suddenly poured in, with more than 60 numbers arriving, totaling more than 9,000 shi of goods, which caused public sentiment to become weak again, and the market color declined. Sales in Qingdao, Weihaiwei, Tianjin, and other groups continued to advance by 700 to 800 bags, but the overall situation was still that the supply exceeded the demand. As a result, the price of thick japonica rice fell by a jiao or so, and the market for late rice was reduced by several fen to nearly a jiao. And various colors such as Du Yangjian and Yin Yuan continued to fall by one or two jiao due to the lack of sales channels.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, 45-6 of He Xia's various goods arrived. The market's various sales of white japonica rice are gradually advancing in packaging, while the sales of loose rice are sluggish. Early thin rice and various sharp changes, Yin Yuan, are also very quiet. The market price of white japonica rice is down by nearly a jiao, and the remaining goods are tired.

Bran is Not Abundant in Stock or Sales

The bran market has been extremely calm in recent days. Although the stock is not very abundant, external dealers have not been active. Only a few sporadic transactions are taking place inland. Prices are slightly weaker than last week, with mixed bran quoted at 2.7 yuan and Fuxin bran quoted at 7.5 jiao.

Sugar Market

The First Tray of New Hainan Red Sugar Has Been Opened

Yesterday, the sugar market was stable. The association's price for No. 24 coarse granulated white spot was 18.4 yuan, and the warehouse goods were 18.5 yuan. The re-export price was 5.2 jiao, and transactions were made at the original price. No. 8 and 9 Dutch red sugar were 14 yuan for ordinary and 14.4 yuan for high No. 9, and the re-export price was 4.9 jiao, with no change. Taikoo Sugar B mark was 19.4 yuan, and the local factory's cotton white Zhenji and Zhenyu No. 1 were still 17.7 yuan. The first batch of 61 bags of new Hainan red sugar arrived. The goods were good and were immediately opened, with a price of 13 yuan. The new Chao Ning arrived from the Suiyang and Hesheng rounds the night before last, with a total of more than 2,100 bags. The dealers, due to the active sales, have a stable trend, so the arrived goods were opened and put into circulation in full. The quotation for the delivery to Qingzhuang was 12.5-6 jiao, Huanggang Qing was 12.3-4 jiao, the next was two jiao, and Hong Kong Qing was 12 yuan. (According to the current sugar stock, there are only more than 20,000 bags of coarse granulated white Dutch red. According to the high trend of yesterday's gold market, the later market may have the possibility of rising, so it is specially noted here to observe its development.) Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talks

Sickness and Medicine

— Field Dweller

If a “Motorcar” breaks down, it needs repair, and if a person gets sick, they need medicine. This is the same “natural law”!

I don’t have the good fortune to sit in a “Motorcar,” and I get sick two or three to five or six times a year. Since that’s the case, then let’s talk about “sickness” and “medicine,” because that’s a more personal issue. Moreover, the rag-picking Xiao Liu Zi will lie on the road and cry about a stomachache, and the “young master” resting on a wild duck down pillow will sometimes get a fever. Sickness for people is just that equal.

Everyone is afraid of getting sick, and taking medicine isn’t exactly welcome either. From children who are “still wet behind the ears” to old men with “white beards and eyebrows,” they all groan when they get sick, and their eyes don’t want to look at people. This shows that being sick is very painful. “Even heroes fear the grind of illness!” If heroes can’t bear it, then ordinary people can forget about enduring it. Therefore, if you’re not sick, then so be it, but if you do get sick, you have to get treated quickly. After all, today’s doctors are all “devoted to saving the world.” For one dollar and twenty cents, they write a prescription, clearly stating your pulse, tongue coating, bowel movements, and whether you have constipation or diarrhea, and they prescribe the amount of licorice and dried tangerine peel. Don’t think that just because the first dose doesn’t work, you should distrust your doctor. It’s said that prudent doctors use the first prescription as a “test of the illness.” Then, they gradually diagnose and treat you with a second, third, fourth, and so on. Although you’ll suffer in bed for a few more days and spend a few more dollars, it’s not a waste because they’re willing to carefully treat you day after day, so you won’t die.

Sick families without cultivation mostly believe in Western medicine because Western medicine is “effective on the spot.” They’ll stick a needle in your thigh, making you scream like a slaughtered pig. If your head feels hot, they’ll give you two ice packs. If your body is cold, they’ll start a fire for you. If your stomach feels uncomfortable, they’ll give you medicine water. Perhaps if you get a boil, they’ll cut out a piece of flesh. Some say this seems too disloyal, but “dying” and “coming back to life” isn’t a bad way to be “straightforward and quick.”

From this perspective, Chinese and Western doctors each have their advantages. I’ve seen sick families invite both Chinese and Western doctors to their homes. This is probably because their family has a lot of money. With one more doctor, their life has one more layer of protection. In the event that they reach a point where the “real illness is hard to cure,” then it’s good to let their descendants say something loud on the “obituary.” After all, the money won’t be spent in vain. However, there’s another group of people who can’t afford to see a doctor when they get sick, and that’s really bad. Although doctors are “devoted to saving the world,” you still have to pay for the rickshaw puller, the maid, and the Western-style house in the shikumen. The famous ones are even more valuable. Even if there are “reduced rates for the poor” or even something like a “commemorative free consultation,” you still can’t swallow the prescription. Isn’t it even worse for a doctor to examine you if there’s no medicine to take? Therefore, some people say that poor people shouldn’t get sick in the first place, and there’s some truth to that.

However, as I said at the beginning, sickness is very fair. Rag pickers and people who sit in “Motorcars” all have the qualifications and opportunities to get sick. However, the issue of seeing a doctor and taking medicine isn’t something everyone can talk about. Therefore, it’s best not to be poor when you’re a person, and if you’re poor, it’s best not to get sick. “Good health is a blessing for the poor.” To hell with “Motorcars

Winter Solstice

— Zhang Yiping

It was his most triumphant year. The South Goods store on East Street closed down due to the owner's death, leaving him as the only store in Wujia Town selling South Goods. Partly it was the encouragement of friends, and partly there was a genuine need for business expansion. When he retrieved the large silver dollars accumulated over the years from copper coins and silver dimes, an uncontrollable joy spread through his body like a snake. They first put up a sign saying "Renovating the facade, business as usual." Every morning, his huge body moved in and out of the store, partly to respond to the customers' congratulations, "Boss, congratulations!", and partly for fear of hindering the carpenters' work. Although it was late autumn and early winter, moisture beaded on his large head. The mischievous children clapped their little hands at his door and shouted, "Steamed buns, two copper coins for one." He always wore a smiling face and gave each child a piece of banana candy.

The facade was newly renovated, and the goods were shipped in. To commemorate the grand opening of the new store, there was a special three-day bargain sale. Before the winter solstice, the place was packed with people every day, and moisture naturally beaded on his large head, but "Boss, Boss," he wished he had more than two hands.

This year, the first business to close in Wujia Town was Dexiang Grocery Store. He took stock of his money and goods, and his big belly swayed even more impressively. Moreover, on New Year's Eve, his footprints were found in the restaurant.

Although everyone in town knew the big fat man, he had never done business in the hotel. The waiter greeted him: "Fat boss, congratulations on your fortune!"

"Haha, may everyone get rich, ha..."

As he moved his body, he nodded to the seated guests.

On the fifth day of the New Year, he welcomed the God of Wealth, and his store was particularly lively. According to rural custom, businesses close for five days during the New Year. After tonight, business would resume tomorrow, so welcoming the God of Wealth was an even bigger event than eating New Year's Eve dinner. The fat man felt that the safety lamp was not bright enough, so he rented a gasoline lamp. Neighbors nearby came to join in the fun. He remembered that he didn't send the guests away until after midnight.

As his usual smiling face unfolded, he was awakened by a shout. A child standing as tall as the counter stood in the store:

"Fat uncle, two copper coins for some white sugar, quick!"

"What's the rush!" He didn't expect his voice to come out so loud.

"My little brother is crying. My older sister is feeding him porridge, but he doesn't want it. She's buying white sugar to feed him sugary porridge," the child innocently replied.

"Where's your mom?"

"Mom went to Shanghai this morning to ask Dad for money."

These words satisfied him. The grievances in his heart seemed to have been expressed to this child. He gave the child goods worth twice the price, waving his hand repeatedly:

"Go back quickly."

The sun was already overhead, and the sunlight in the store had receded to the center of the street. The black dog was sleeping soundly on the steps again. He raised his big head and looked at the calendar on the wall, muttering:

"Today is the eighteenth. Tomorrow, the day after tomorrow, the day after the day after tomorrow is the winter solstice!" (The End)

A Daughter Belongs to Another Family

— (Rural Sketch)

Spider

— Lu Yan

As long as it is sunny, you can see spiders weaving their webs in the corners of houses, especially after a storm in the summer. However, in the city, with such magnificent high-rise buildings, so spotless and truly "flawless," where can you find a trace of spiders? Here, we must deeply lament for the spiders who weave their own nets, cleverly set traps, and capture small flying insects!

Even if they occasionally come to second-class buildings, it is only a fleeting moment, as they will be banished to oblivion by the servants. The fate of spiders in the high-rise buildings of the city is that their tracks are rarely seen. However, in such a dilapidated house, it seems that its fate will soon be eliminated. Moreover, in this ever-changing city, under the concept of "every inch of land is worth gold," it is inevitable that they will be targeted by people seeking profit. Naturally, living here is because the rent is cheaper, and the atmosphere is outdated. Modern city dwellers (except for another kind of person) cannot stand it. For this reason, they are naturally ridiculed. Therefore, in this dilapidated house, it goes without saying that in better locations, or like in a dark corner of the wall, with a sliver of light, near where people live, there is naturally a spider's graceful presence. She weaves her web there, waiting for small flying insects to fly into it. However, the small flying insects fly into the net not out of any bad intentions, but because they want to find a way out, because everyone loves the light. Being trapped in the darkness is what no one wants, unless it is another kind of thing.

In this situation, I happened to see a spider hanging down from a crack in a small house. At the same time, it released strands of silk that drifted with the wind. It seemed that its purpose was to secure itself to something. With the help of the air, it became even more rampant. After all, there was nothing for it to bind to in the empty surroundings, but time and space are dynamic. There are various forms in every second, even if we cannot see them all at once. However, it was too arrogant. Without paying attention, a sudden gust of wind blew down a fallen leaf, which happened to fall on its web. In such a dilapidated state, it naturally broke. Without caring, it walked back onto its broken web, picked up the remnants of the damaged net, and reorganized its new web, spinning vigorously as it did its work. Before long, in the small gap where the light came in, it had woven a new web. It was ready for the small flying insects to fly into it.

I couldn't help but think of her full of plans. Setting up her web in a very suitable place would allow her to obtain the victory she needed. That's right, this is an opportunity, and she understood this opportunity. The small flying insects were completely oblivious. She took advantage of a sliver of light, anticipating that the small flying insects would go to the light. The light is naturally a great sky, where they can soar freely. Here, she had a very good opportunity. In this accidental feeling, I understood this side of life, and then I understood the speculators!

Killing a Chicken

— Chen Liang

In an overly lonely state, a kind of fantasy often emerges from a clear mind. Even a common thing that people don't pay attention to often lingers in sensitive thoughts and leads to extraordinary insights. I observe everything carefully, from a tiny ant to a huge elephant, from a spark to the raging flames in a boiler, with the same eyes and thoughts. Recently, I suddenly had a perverse whim: to see a tragic scene of killing, but at the same time, I didn't want to get this opportunity too easily. Although I am not a timid or idealistic person, I can't bear to see a fresh, lively life suddenly fall on its own stream of hot blood!

Speaking of watching the killing of a chicken this time, it took the courage of going to an execution ground.

This morning, there was a bright sky outside the skylight. Two rays of sunlight squeezed in through the cracks in the wall and licked the white curtains, licking them into two circles of brilliant light. I love the morning air, so I got up and got out of bed. Just as I was about to go for a walk in the nearby park, an unfamiliar fellow countryman came with two chickens in his hand. At first, I was very suspicious, but later I learned that a relative in the countryside had asked him to bring them to me. So, after I sent the fellow countryman out the door, a problem lay before me waiting to be solved. The problem was the two chickens. "Having a few more friends in my not-so-spacious room carries the risk of stepping on each other's frostbite. How can I raise chickens! Moreover, chicken droppings all over the floor are a hindrance to both hygiene and appearance. How should I deal with them?" I leaned back on the sofa and pondered for a cigarette's time.

"Give them to a friend, but I don't want to use animal life as a gift to show my goodwill to others. Although in today's society, people's lives are often given as gifts to each other, I still maintain this unique idea. Isn't that too stupid? But, for me, it is a principle that must be maintained. I would rather kill, cook, and eat these two chickens myself. I don't want to use them to flatter and bribe others in order to gain some extra benefits." So, when I dropped the second cigarette butt, I had a solution to the problem: "I'll just kill them and eat them myself!" Thus, the scene of killing the chicken unfolded!

The second landlord's helper was a skilled chicken killer and was willing to do it for me. He familiarly bent the neck of the female chicken towards its wings. I was already a little chilly, but reason told myself, "It is a creature that is eaten by people anyway." But watching him pluck the feathers around the throat, revealing the peach-colored skin, the female chicken's legs and claws also began to shake, knowing that she was feeling pain, I couldn't bear it. I regretted not giving it away, but reason told myself, "She also pecked at insects when she was alive," so I watched the bright blade plunging into the peach-colored skin, and when the blood flowed straight out, I almost wanted to hide.

The male chicken was also caught by the helper while running away, and he bent its neck, plucked its feathers, and wielded the knife, and blood flowed in the same way.

Two fresh, lively lives were destroyed in an instant. From this perverse situation, I thought of the execution ground, and from killing the chicken, I imagined killing people. I raised my head, and it was a clear sky.

Amateur Mailbox

What to do When I Can't Attend Night School!

Editor:

Since the summer vacation of my fifteenth year, I have been forced by circumstances to abandon my books and become an apprentice in a store in this city. This year, I have finally finished my apprenticeship.

Now I feel that my knowledge is very shallow, and when I think about my future prospects, there is really no bright hope. Every night, watching people carrying books to night school to study and seek advanced knowledge, I am very envious. So I have repeatedly asked my boss to allow me to read for two hours at night. But my boss is a thorough conservative with feudal ideas, not only refusing my request but also threatening to stop my business. Although I have been rejected several times, my desire to study has not diminished.

Recently, I have come up with many methods, but I cannot achieve the goal of studying at night. It really makes me extremely sad!

Page 19

Sir, you are a mentor to young people like me. Please tell me a way to deepen my knowledge! I wish you

Well-being, Hu Jing

Editor's Note: It is indeed the most painful thing in the world to have an extremely high desire for knowledge but not be able to satisfy it. However, most old-fashioned store owners cannot understand the meaning and importance of learning, so Mr. Hu was refused by his boss for wanting to attend night school. We believe that looking at this phenomenon in Shanghai alone, the number of young people who feel as troubled as Mr. Hu is countless. Not to mention the interior.

Now Mr. Hu should continue to work hard and ask someone related to the store owner and with a clear mind to speak on his behalf. The words should be tactful and pleasant to reach the goal of learning.

If this step is also difficult to achieve, we advise Mr. Hu not to be too discouraged, thinking that there is no hope for learning. He can secretly entrust someone to find a better opportunity and try to get rid of the boss's constraints. On the other hand, he should think of other ways to satisfy his desire for knowledge.

Regarding the method of learning, we believe that it is certainly better to go to school, but if the environment does not allow it and there is no such opportunity, you can also obtain the knowledge you need without going to school. Going to day school or night school is just to get a little tool knowledge. To acquire advanced knowledge, you must rely on your own efforts, which cannot be obtained solely from school. Therefore, we advise Mr. Hu not to be disappointed. He should make the greatest determination and use his spare time to carry out self-study. Dedicating himself to studying whenever he has a little time, with years of effort, his knowledge will increase imperceptibly.

This newspaper has established a circulating library on the third floor of the Continental Commercial Building, providing books suitable for the general uneducated, without charging readers any fees. It has also established a reading guidance department to solve readers' questions about books as much as possible. Mr. Hu, if you intend to study on your own, can join the library. For detailed information and procedures, please contact the library directly to inquire about everything.

Ballad Singing

Chen Ruilin, Mao Jiazhe

Yuan Chang (1120) 5:30 PM to 6:15 PM

Opening Piece "Nonsense About the Imperial Examination"

Osmanthus fragrance fills the shade of trees. The battlefield of literature is the same everywhere. Old events are revisited with many sighs. Nonsense about the imperial examination is full of fun. The new words are compiled into strings and frets again. How can old dreams bear the rain and dew? Relatives and friends send examination boxes one after another. Osmanthus rounds and lotus seeds have the same meaning. There is also a good wish. Continuous success is spoken of in the autumn wind. Temporary shops on Qingyun Street. All kinds of goods are sold at public prices. Ladies and gentlemen gather like a city. Shoulders rub and wheels knock, making the road difficult to pass. Each official examiner enters with thorn barriers. Strict defense is not willing to loosen. Wooden benches and cloth curtains are prepared by themselves. Careful preparation is endless. (There are also) Qingyun ladders and various uses. Auspicious words are double-related in the tube. The examination sedan travels quickly without curtains. The examination tools are carried in the east and west. They ask if the scholar must pass. The good news of the name is heard in the sedan. The morning light is slightly revealed, and the rooster crows three times. At the fifth watch, the roll call is sleepy-eyed. Lantern signs are divided left and right. Ten thousand people enter in an orderly manner. The signed card is held in hand and hurriedly entered. The examination basket is carried on the back and the chest heaves. The thin and timid body is difficult to walk. The bitterness is full of resentment. The examination rooms are lined up like wild geese. The words "cosmos, flood, wilderness" are all understood. They recognize their seat numbers. The tents are hung up and it is lively and bustling. A battle on the literary field builds a miracle.

Zhou Jianhong, Red Robe

Zhong Xi (1040) 11:45 PM to 12:30 AM

Opening Piece "Modern Female Painter"

Women in the world are now skilled in painting. They have inherited the original skills of imitation. Wu Qingxia's wonderful brushwork creates figures. Flowers and feathers are all capable. Gu Qingyao's ancestor, Ruobo, passed on wonderful brushwork. Southern landscape painting studies Hua Ting. Lu Xiaoman studies the six laws of landscape painting. Her unparalleled intelligence is in her brushwork. She inherits the mantle of Bai Long, Yang Xijiu. Li Qiujun is also skilled in calligraphy and painting. Yu Tanhan learns from Sheng Yuan, Wang's brushwork. Both north and south are skilled and praised in the art world. Jiang Yanan is skilled in dyeing and writing. Her youthful landscape paintings have gained a good name. Zhang Hongwei's flowers and birds are unmatched. He is the successor of Yun Shui. The Wang sisters are female painters. In addition to Leng Ying, there is also Qing Ying. Zhang Shimin's insects, flowers, and birds can all be written. They can be counted as vivid and fragrant. Only a few talented women are uncountable. The art world is well-regarded. I wish them fame in the painting world throughout Spring City.

Ms. Wang Bingmei's Tang Poetry

Hua Xing (1260) 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM

Choubi Post Station Li Shangyin

Monkeys and birds still fear the written orders, the wind and clouds often protect the storage place.

It only makes the general wield his divine pen, and finally sees the surrendered king running in a passing carriage.

Guan Zhong and Yue Yi had talent but were not ambitious, what could Guan Yu and Zhang Fei do without destiny?

In later years, passing through the ancestral hall in Jinli, the Liang Fu chant became full of regret.

Untitled Li Shangyin

It's hard to meet and hard to part, the east wind is weak and the flowers are withered.

The silkworm spins silk until it dies, the candle burns to ashes and the tears begin to dry.

In the morning, the mirror only worries about the change of sideburns, and at night, chanting should feel the moonlight cold.

It is not far from the lotus platform, and the blue bird diligently explores and looks.

Spring Rain Li Shangyin

Sadly lying in new spring white clothes, the White Gate is desolate and the meaning is mostly contrary.

The red building is separated by rain and looks coldly at each other, the beaded curtains drift and the lights return alone.

The long road should grieve over the late spring, and the remaining night still dreams faintly.

How can the jade earring be delivered? Ten thousand miles of clouds surround a wild goose flying.

Shen Bao Architectural Weekly

New Trends in American Architecture

— Qin

Before the World War, Americans, relying on their wealth and material progress, were obsessed with tall buildings, competing and boasting with each other. In prosperous cities such as New York and Chicago, due to the high land prices and large populations, the rise of tall buildings was a natural and inevitable result of the environment. A famous American architect once said, "Because of the system of tall buildings, a businessman in New York City can conduct five times more meetings and negotiations in one morning than in London or Paris." From this, we can see how important this commercial convenience is in today's economically developed society.

High land prices and large populations are not the only reasons for the rise of tall buildings. We can say that the curiosity and vanity of Americans are a driving force for success. At the same time, the development of American engineering and the abundance and cheapness of materials are also major factors. For example, although Americans were able to build 500-foot-tall buildings thanks to the convenience of electric elevators, if engineers had not invented the simultaneous use of two elevators on the same shaft, then 1,000-foot-tall buildings would have faced difficulties in elevator transportation.

The architecture of the "Old World," those buildings taller than five or six stories, were merely extensions of previous architecture. The tall buildings on Fifth Avenue in New York had twelve stories, which was considered a great feat at the time. However, we see that its cornices still followed the old style, pre-carved and installed. Its usefulness was insufficient to cover even a small part of the wall, and compared to the entire building, its size seemed even more discordant, making people laugh.

As buildings gradually increased in height, this Italian palace-style construction method was abandoned, and the use of steel frames flourished. The Woolworth Building in New York City is a large project that Americans boast about. Its straight-line steel frame is very magnificent. However, this was only a slight improvement over the past. American architects still couldn't help but use spires, church-style roofs, niches, pilasters, and Gothic-style ornaments, which, besides giving people a religious impression, had no meaning whatsoever. Later, other tall buildings were erected, and although they did not entirely carry the remnants of the past, they still inevitably retained some traces of antiquity at the base and roof.

At this time, Americans felt a strong interest in tall buildings, and municipal and residential hygiene were also greatly affected. Therefore, New York had a new law called the "Zoning Law." This law not only restricted the height of buildings but also restricted the style of architecture. Generally speaking, this law stipulates that builders are only allowed to build buildings of any height on a portion of their entire land, and the height of other street-facing portions must not exceed several times the street width, with the ratio depending on the area. This means that in some areas, the height of street-facing buildings must not exceed 200 feet, and in some areas, it must not exceed 250 feet. Beyond this, the building should gradually slope inward so that sunlight and air can reach the bottom of the building. As a result, many large buildings, such as the New York Telephone Company Building and the Sherry-Netherland Hotel, were built in succession, all subject to the provisions of this law. The design of the windows of these buildings is quite different from the ordinary, smaller and densely arranged, appearing like spots from a distance. Moreover, the entire building does not have any ancient decorations, making American architecture a new school to this point.

This is the new trend in American architecture. Architects pay attention to engineering design, interior lighting work, and the planning of light and air on the streets around the building. Someone said that today's architects are like sculptors, who can complete any style of building. This statement seems to be quite true, because we now have steel-frame concrete construction methods, strong and light materials never seen before in the world, and countless new engineering equipment. The form of the building is simply not difficult to construct. Therefore, today's architects often make a clay or wax model during the design process, arbitrarily arranging it to achieve the matching they envision. How is this different from the art of sculpture?

Due to the legal restrictions on tall buildings, the taller the building, the larger the ground area occupied at the bottom, and the independence of each building becomes more obvious. After the city is filled with tall buildings, we will no longer see connected buildings standing side by side. The shapes of the buildings are also novel and different. Some can be called steel and glass buildings, some are wrapped in shining metal panels, some are entirely black, and some are as white as snow. There is no commonality in between. Ancient Greek, Roman, and Gothic architecture could not escape many common features, and the efforts of architects seemed limited, but this is not the case with modern architecture. People's minds can also be free and unrestrained, each seeking possible progress in art. This new trend makes American architecture a very promising new development in the world, containing the spirit of freedom and independence in architecture.

Talking About Skyscrapers

— Yingdai

(1) What is a skyscraper?

The so-called skyscraper is a building that seems to scrape the sky. Its summit is so high that it looks like it is touching the top of the sky. "Scraping the sky" is used to describe its height reaching into the clouds. The sky has no top, so how can it be scraped? Therefore, the height of a building cannot truly scrape the sky. Recently, a 22-story skyscraper has been completed in Shanghai. For a time, the names of the International Hotel and the Joint Savings Society were spread by word of mouth. Everyone in the streets and alleys talked about skyscrapers. In fact, everyone, including women and children, knew about it. This 22-story skyscraper, the tallest in East Asia, can indeed proudly show off in the Eastern Hemisphere. In fact, a 22-story skyscraper dominates one side in East Asia, but in European and American countries, it is still a short and low building. Haven't you heard that in London, England, and New York, USA, skyscrapers are as high as fifty or sixty stories? So, why is a 22-story skyscraper worth bragging about? Only because it is the first of its kind in the Far East, it gets talked about far and wide.

(2) Why build skyscrapers?

Some say that two or three stories, or even five or six stories, are enough. Why build twenty or thirty stories? You don't know that the population in cities is increasing day by day, and land prices are rising. In busy places, houses stand close together, and there is a disaster of overcrowding. Therefore, landowners have no other way to remedy this except to increase the number of stories in their buildings to meet the needs of residents. Increasing the height of buildings is of great benefit to landowners. Among buildings, high-rise buildings, so-called skyscrapers, are the most economical to build. Building one story has the same land value as building twenty or thirty stories. This is one reason. The higher the building, the more rooms there will be. The rent received will be more than one story. This is the second reason. During construction, the average construction cost per floor is much cheaper than low-rise buildings. This is the third reason. There are other economic advantages, but I won't go into them all here. Understanding this, the construction of skyscrapers can be roughly understood.

(3) The application of skyscrapers

The construction of skyscrapers is economical for landowners to fully utilize the value of their land, and it can also meet the needs of society to avoid the problem of overcrowding. The use of skyscrapers can be for special shopping malls or for residential accommodation. However, there are also special disadvantages. Opening a store, customers find it inconvenient to go up and down. Living in a skyscraper also has the same suffering. Therefore, unless necessary, skyscrapers may not be suitable for general needs. Taking Shanghai as an example, although the population has exceeded three million, there is still plenty of open space, and most of the houses are two or three stories. Therefore, even if there is overcrowding, adding a third or fourth floor to the residence is enough. Looking at the buildings built recently, most of them are already three or four stories. This is also the reason. However, according to the habits of residents, even three or four-story buildings are inconvenient. How much more so for ten stories or more? Although there are elevators, they will not be happy. The unsuitability of skyscrapers for residential use in Shanghai is evident from this. However, they can still be used for special commercial applications.

(4) The foundation of skyscrapers

When building a skyscraper, the first thing we must pay attention to is the softness or hardness of the foundation and how much weight it can bear. If it cannot bear the weight, the foundation will inevitably sink when the building is high. In New York, USA, the underground is all stone, so skyscrapers, even if they are as high as fifty or sixty stories, will not sink. As for Shanghai, the geology is different. It is close to the coast, and the soil is loose. Therefore, for skyscrapers with more than ten stories, the foundation must be particularly strong, otherwise it cannot bear this weight. Therefore, engineers must regard how the foundation can be made particularly strong and able to bear multi-story buildings as a prerequisite before constructing a skyscraper. The foundation is strong, and then construction can proceed.

(5) The construction of skyscrapers

When building a skyscraper, in addition to paying special attention to the foundation, there are many other points that should be paid attention to during construction. For example, the building materials. In order to ensure the durability and load-bearing capacity of the building, all raw materials must be of high quality. After the building is high, the lower floors often lack light. However, if the construction is done properly, it can also be made to have sufficient light everywhere. In addition, the building is high, there must be many rooms and many people living in it. Therefore, if a fire occurs carelessly, it is not easy to extinguish, especially on the upper floors. If it is unfortunately destroyed by fire, the loss is greater than ordinary houses. Therefore, fire prevention equipment must be thorough. In order to make it convenient and quick for residents to go up and down, elevators should be installed more. In addition, high-rise houses are subject to more severe wind and rain. The windows and glass must be shatterproof, and more walkways must be drawn to facilitate access to toilets, etc. There are too many problems to list. Due to space limitations, I cannot describe them all here.

Architectural Jargon

— Mei Zhenhuan

丨丨About the Usage in Construction Sites丨丨

In the construction of houses, from the perspective of construction, whether it is the method or the materials used, the names of some places are not easily heard by outsiders. It seems that this is a kind of "slang" specially used in construction sites. Now I will write down some of the common words that should be used:

Leveling Water丨丨 Using a surveying instrument (Transit) on uneven ground, small stakes are driven in. (Called leveling stakes) High and low marks are drawn to prevent the building from tilting during construction.

Applying Lime Lines丨丨 Preliminary procedure, carefully considering the dimensions, openings, etc. of the house style on the drawings, such as courtyards, living rooms, and kitchens, under the supervision of the supervisor, pull each linen thread, and then flick it with lime powder (lime powder) to make it appear on the construction site of the house.

Preparing Mortar丨丨 What is called preparing mortar? This is used when building ordinary street houses or lane houses, and laying three-in-one soil (Lime Concrete) after excavating the wall trench (Trench), because three-in-one soil is a basic procedure in ordinary construction and must be compacted into a solid with a heavy stone hammer. Pouring mortar at that time is like mixing some gelatin into the three-in-one soil. Its composition is one part lime and two parts black sand.

Returning Fire丨丨 After compacting the three-in-one soil, compact it twice back and forth. The second time is called returning fire. This is mostly used by Jiangbei construction workers.

Tightening the Waistband丨丨 Another procedure after compacting the three-in-one soil, sprinkle yellow sand on the surface of the three-in-one soil and compact it with a stone hammer. This means tightening the waistband.

Setting the Footing丨丨 Setting the footing is the work of masons. Generally, when building five-inch or ten-inch walls in buildings, the large square footing is set on the three-in-one soil. (Footing) It is gradually reduced, roughly 20 inches, 25 inches, or 30 inches.

Plumbing the Line丨丨 This is also the work of masons. When building a wall every three or five layers, pull the linen thread tightly into a straight line, and then build one brick after another according to the straight line. This is a method to resist the thickness of the bricks and prevent the collapse of the wall.

Killing Ash丨丨 If the mason's skills are not high, the bricks often do not line up when building a wall. The reason is that they are addicted to not plumbing the line. The remedy is to scrape the mortar thinner in the high places, which is called killing ash. Conversely, in the low places, the mortar is thickened, which is called adding ash.

Filling the Trough丨丨 (Flush) Also known as scraping the trough, the mortar is applied to each layer of bricks.

Pointing丨丨 Means to clean the mortar joints (Pointing).

Eight-tenths Short丨丨 A brick that is two-tenths short is called eight-tenths short.

Broody Hen丨丨 Not the broody hen in animals, but the switch on the hammer used for driving piles. The shape is very similar to that of a broody hen.

Shrinkage丨丨 (Shrink) Wood is easy to shrink when wet and expand when heated. The meaning of shrinkage is like this.

Dotted Line丨丨 (Dotted Line) It is a black line on the drawing that is not used for building the house, but is drawn on the drawing one by one. This is called a dotted line.

Trestle丨丨 Trestle (Trestil) is used to mark the thickness of the dimensions and to support the scaffolding when ramming cement (Cement).

Joint丨丨 Where the wall body and the wall body are connected, inlaid with dog-tooth-like bricks, it is called joint (Bond). It has female (Groove) and male (Toothing) differences.

Rabbet丨丨 The width of the wall body, if the bricks are difficult to match, you can leave some gaps in the middle, this gap is called rabbet (Rebate). (To be continued)
